<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-332">Um texto literal diferente dos parâmetros de rota (por exemplo, `{id}`) e do separador de caminho `/` precisa corresponder ao texto na URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-332">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-333">A correspondência de texto não diferencia maiúsculas de minúsculas e se baseia na representação decodificada do caminho de URLs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-333">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URLs path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-334">Para encontrar a correspondência de um delimitador de parâmetro de rota literal (`{` ou `}`), faça o escape do delimitador repetindo o caractere (`{{` ou `}}`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-334">To match a literal route parameter delimiter (`{` or `}`), escape the delimiter by repeating the character (`{{` or `}}`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-335">Padrões de URL que tentam capturar um nome de arquivo com uma extensão de arquivo opcional apresentam considerações adicionais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-335">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-336">Por exemplo, considere o modelo `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-336">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-337">Quando existem valores para `filename` e `ext`, ambos os valores são populados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-337">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-338">Se apenas existir um valor para `filename` na URL, a rota encontrará uma correspondência, pois o ponto à direita (`.`) é opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-338">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing period (`.`) is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-339">As URLs a seguir correspondem a essa rota:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-339">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-340">Você pode usar um asterisco (`*`) ou um asterisco duplo (`**`) como um prefixo para um parâmetro de rota para associá-lo ao restante do URI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-340">You can use an asterisk (`*`) or double asterisk (`**`) as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-341">Eles são chamados de parâmetros *catch-all*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-341">These are called a *catch-all* parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-342">Por exemplo, `blog/{**slug}` corresponde a qualquer URI que começa com `/blog` e tem qualquer valor depois dele, que é atribuído ao valor de rota `slug`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-342">For example, `blog/{**slug}` matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it, which is assigned to the `slug` route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-343">Os parâmetros catch-all também podem corresponder à cadeia de caracteres vazia.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-343">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-344">O parâmetro catch-all faz o escape dos caracteres corretos quando a rota é usada para gerar uma URL, incluindo os caracteres separadores de caminho (`/`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-344">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator (`/`) characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-345">Por exemplo, a rota `foo/{*path}` com valores de rota `{ path = "my/path" }` gera `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-345">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-346">Observe o escape da barra invertida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-346">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-347">Para fazer a viagem de ida e volta dos caracteres separadores de caminho, use o prefixo do parâmetro da rota `**`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-347">To round-trip path separator characters, use the `**` route parameter prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-348">A rota `foo/{**path}` com `{ path = "my/path" }` gera `foo/my/path`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-348">The route `foo/{**path}` with `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my/path`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-349">Os parâmetros de rota podem ter *valores padrão*, designados pela especificação do valor padrão após o nome do parâmetro separado por um sinal de igual (`=`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-349">Route parameters may have *default values* designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-350">Por exemplo, `{controller=Home}` define `Home` como o valor padrão de `controller`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-350">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-351">O valor padrão é usado se nenhum valor está presente na URL para o parâmetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-351">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-352">Os parâmetros de rota se tornam opcionais com o acréscimo de um ponto de interrogação (`?`) ao final do nome do parâmetro, como em `id?`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-352">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name, as in `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-353">A diferença entre valores opcionais e parâmetros de rota padrão é que um parâmetro de rota com um valor padrão sempre produz um valor – um parâmetro opcional tem um valor somente quando um valor é fornecido pela URL de solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-353">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is that a route parameter with a default value always produces a value&mdash;an optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-354">Os parâmetros de rota podem ter restrições que precisam corresponder ao valor de rota associado da URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-354">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-355">A adição de dois-pontos (`:`) e do nome da restrição após o nome do parâmetro de rota especifica uma *restrição embutida* em um parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-355">Adding a colon (`:`) and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an *inline constraint* on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-356">Se a restrição exigir argumentos, eles ficarão entre parênteses (`(...)`) após o nome da restrição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-356">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses (`(...)`) after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-357">Várias restrições embutidas podem ser especificadas por meio do acréscimo de outros dois-pontos (`:`) e do nome da restrição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-357">Multiple inline constraints can be specified by appending another colon (`:`) and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-358">O nome da restrição e os argumentos são passados para o serviço <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> para criar uma instância de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> a ser usada no processamento de URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-358">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-359">Por exemplo, o modelo de rota `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` especifica uma restrição `minlength` com o argumento `10`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-359">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-360">Para obter mais informações sobre as restrições de rota e uma lista das restrições fornecidas pela estrutura, confira a seção [Referência de restrição de rota](#route-constraint-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-360">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-361">Os parâmetros de rota também podem ter transformadores de parâmetro, que transformam o valor de um parâmetro ao gerar links e fazer a correspondência de ações e páginas com URLs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-361">Route parameters may also have parameter transformers, which transform a parameter's value when generating links and matching actions and pages to URLs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-362">Assim como as restrições, os transformadores de parâmetro podem ser adicionados embutidos a um parâmetro de rota colocando dois-pontos (`:`) e o nome do transformador após o nome do parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-362">Like constraints, parameter transformers can be added inline to a route parameter by adding a colon (`:`) and transformer name after the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-363">Por exemplo, o modelo de rota `blog/{article:slugify}` especifica um transformador `slugify`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-363">For example, the route template `blog/{article:slugify}` specifies a `slugify` transformer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-364">Para obter mais informações sobre transformadores de parâmetro, confira a seção [Referência de transformador de parâmetro](#parameter-transformer-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-364">For more information on parameter transformers, see the [Parameter transformer reference](#parameter-transformer-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-365">A tabela a seguir demonstra modelos de rota de exemplo e seu comportamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-365">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-366">Modelo de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-366">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-367">URI de correspondência de exemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-367">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-368">O URI de solicitação&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-368">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-369">Somente corresponde ao caminho único `/hello`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-369">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-370">Faz a correspondência e define `Page` como `Home`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-370">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-371">Faz a correspondência e define `Page` como `Contact`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-371">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-372">É mapeado para o controlador `Products` e a ação `List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-372">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-373">É mapeado para o controlador `Products` e a ação `Details` (`id` definido como 123).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-373">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action (`id` set to 123).</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-374">É mapeado para o controlador `Home` e o método `Index` (`id` é ignorado).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-374">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method (`id` is ignored).</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-375">Em geral, o uso de um modelo é a abordagem mais simples para o roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-375">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-376">Restrições e padrões também podem ser especificados fora do modelo de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-376">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-377">Habilite o [Log](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) para ver como as implementações de roteamento internas, como <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, correspondem às solicitações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-377">Enable [Logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) to see how the built-in routing implementations, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, match requests.</span></span>

## <a name="reserved-routing-names"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-378">Nomes reservados de roteamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-378">Reserved routing names</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-379">As seguintes palavras-chave são nomes reservados e não podem ser usadas como nomes de rota ou parâmetros:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-379">The following keywords are reserved names and can't be used as route names or parameters:</span></span>

* `action`
* `area`
* `controller`
* `handler`
* `page`

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-380">Referência de restrição de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-380">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-381">As restrições de rota são executadas quando ocorre uma correspondência com a URL de entrada e é criado um token do caminho da URL em valores de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-381">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-382">Em geral, as restrições da rota inspecionam o valor de rota associado por meio do modelo de rota e tomam uma decisão do tipo "sim/não" sobre se o valor é aceitável ou não.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-382">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a yes/no decision about whether or not the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-383">Algumas restrições da rota usam dados fora do valor de rota para considerar se a solicitação pode ser encaminhada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-383">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-384">Por exemplo, a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> pode aceitar ou rejeitar uma solicitação de acordo com o verbo HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-384">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-385">As restrições são usadas em solicitações de roteamento e na geração de link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-385">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-386">Não use restrições para a **validação de entrada**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-386">Don't use constraints for **input validation**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-387">Se as restrições forem usadas para a **validação de entrada**, uma entrada inválida resultará em uma resposta *404 – Não Encontrado*, em vez de *400 – Solicitação Inválida* com uma mensagem de erro apropriada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-387">If constraints are used for **input validation**, invalid input results in a *404 - Not Found* response instead of a *400 - Bad Request* with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-388">As restrições de rota são usadas para **desfazer a ambiguidade** entre rotas semelhantes, não para validar as entradas de uma rota específica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-388">Route constraints are used to **disambiguate** similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-389">A tabela a seguir demonstra restrições de rota de exemplo e seu comportamento esperado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-389">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-390">restrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-390">constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-391">Exemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-391">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-392">Correspondências de exemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-392">Example Matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-393">Observações</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-393">Notes</span></span> |
| ---------- | ------- | --------------- | ----- |
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-394">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-394">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-395">Corresponde a qualquer inteiro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-395">Matches any integer</span></span> |
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-396">`true`, `FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-396">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-397">Corresponde a `true` ou `false` (não diferencia maiúsculas de minúsculas)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-397">Matches `true` or `false` (case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-398">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-398">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-399">Corresponde a um valor `DateTime` válido (na cultura invariável – veja o aviso)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-399">Matches a valid `DateTime` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `decimal` | `{price:decimal}` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-400">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-400">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-401">Corresponde a um valor `decimal` válido (na cultura invariável – veja o aviso)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-401">Matches a valid `decimal` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `double` | `{weight:double}` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-402">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-402">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-403">Corresponde a um valor `double` válido (na cultura invariável – veja o aviso)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-403">Matches a valid `double` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `float` | `{weight:float}` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-404">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-404">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-405">Corresponde a um valor `float` válido (na cultura invariável – veja o aviso)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-405">Matches a valid `float` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `guid` | `{id:guid}` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-406">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-406">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-407">Corresponde a um valor `Guid` válido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-407">Matches a valid `Guid` value</span></span> |
| `long` | `{ticks:long}` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-408">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-408">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-409">Corresponde a um valor `long` válido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-409">Matches a valid `long` value</span></span> |
| `minlength(value)` | `{username:minlength(4)}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-410">A cadeia de caracteres deve ter, no mínimo, 4 caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-410">String must be at least 4 characters</span></span> |
| `maxlength(value)` | `{filename:maxlength(8)}` | `Richard` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-411">A cadeia de caracteres não pode ser maior que 8 caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-411">String must be no more than 8 characters</span></span> |
| `length(length)` | `{filename:length(12)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-412">A cadeia de caracteres deve ter exatamente 12 caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-412">String must be exactly 12 characters long</span></span> |
| `length(min,max)` | `{filename:length(8,16)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-413">A cadeia de caracteres deve ter, pelo menos, 8 e não mais de 16 caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-413">String must be at least 8 and no more than 16 characters long</span></span> |
| `min(value)` | `{age:min(18)}` | `19` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-414">O valor inteiro deve ser, pelo menos, 18</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-414">Integer value must be at least 18</span></span> |
| `max(value)` | `{age:max(120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-415">O valor inteiro não deve ser maior que 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-415">Integer value must be no more than 120</span></span> |
| `range(min,max)` | `{age:range(18,120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-416">O valor inteiro deve ser, pelo menos, 18, mas não maior que 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-416">Integer value must be at least 18 but no more than 120</span></span> |
| `alpha` | `{name:alpha}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-417">A cadeia de caracteres deve consistir em um ou mais caracteres alfabéticos (`a`-`z`, não diferencia maiúsculas de minúsculas)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-417">String must consist of one or more alphabetical characters (`a`-`z`, case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-418">A cadeia de caracteres deve corresponder à expressão regular (veja as dicas sobre como definir uma expressão regular)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-418">String must match the regular expression (see tips about defining a regular expression)</span></span> |
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-419">Usado para impor que um valor não parâmetro está presente durante a geração de URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-419">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-420">Várias restrições delimitadas por dois-pontos podem ser aplicadas a um único parâmetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-420">Multiple, colon-delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-421">Por exemplo, a restrição a seguir restringe um parâmetro para um valor inteiro de 1 ou maior:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-421">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-422">As restrições de rota que verificam a URL e são convertidas em um tipo CLR (como `int` ou `DateTime`) sempre usam a cultura invariável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-422">Route constraints that verify the URL and are converted to a CLR type (such as `int` or `DateTime`) always use the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-423">Essas restrições consideram que a URL não é localizável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-423">These constraints assume that the URL is non-localizable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-424">As restrições de rota fornecidas pela estrutura não modificam os valores armazenados nos valores de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-424">The framework-provided route constraints don't modify the values stored in route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-425">Todos os valores de rota analisados com base na URL são armazenados como cadeias de caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-425">All route values parsed from the URL are stored as strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-426">Por exemplo, a restrição `float` tenta converter o valor de rota em um float, mas o valor convertido é usado somente para verificar se ele pode ser convertido em um float.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-426">For example, the `float` constraint attempts to convert the route value to a float, but the converted value is used only to verify it can be converted to a float.</span></span>

## <a name="regular-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-427">Expressões regulares</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-427">Regular expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-428">A estrutura do ASP.NET Core adiciona `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` ao construtor de expressão regular.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-428">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-429">Confira <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> para obter uma descrição desses membros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-429">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-430">As expressões regulares usam delimitadores e tokens semelhantes aos usados pelo Roteamento e pela linguagem C#.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-430">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by Routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-431">Os tokens de expressão regular precisam ter escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-431">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-432">Para usar a expressão regular `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` no roteamento, a expressão precisa ter os caracteres `\` (barra invertida) fornecidos na cadeia de caracteres como caracteres `\\` (barra invertida dupla) no arquivo de origem C# para fazer o escape do caractere de escape da cadeia de caracteres `\` (a menos que estejam sendo usados [literais de cadeia de caracteres textuais](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-432">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in routing, the expression must have the `\` (single backslash) characters provided in the string as `\\` (double backslash) characters in the C# source file in order to escape the `\` string escape character (unless using [verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-433">Para fazer o escape dos caracteres de delimitador de parâmetro de roteamento (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), duplique os caracteres na expressão (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-433">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), double the characters in the expression (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-434">A tabela a seguir mostra uma expressão regular e a versão com escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-434">The following table shows a regular expression and the escaped version.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-435">Expressão regular</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-435">Regular Expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-436">Expressão regular com escape</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-436">Escaped Regular Expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-437">As expressões regulares usadas no roteamento geralmente começam com o caractere de acento circunflexo (`^`) e correspondem à posição inicial da cadeia de caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-437">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the caret (`^`) character and match starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-438">As expressões geralmente terminam com o caractere de cifrão (`$`) e correspondem ao final da cadeia de caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-438">The expressions often end with the dollar sign (`$`) character and match end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-439">Os caracteres `^` e `$` garantem que a expressão regular corresponde a todo o valor do parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-439">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression match the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-440">Sem os caracteres `^` e `$`, a expressão regular corresponde a qualquer subcadeia de caracteres na cadeia de caracteres, o que geralmente não é o desejado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-440">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression match any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-441">A tabela a seguir fornece exemplos e explica por que eles encontram ou não uma correspondência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-441">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-442">Expressão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-442">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-443">Cadeia de Caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-443">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-444">Corresponder a</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-444">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-445">Comentário</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-445">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-446">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-446">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-447">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-447">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-448">A subcadeia de caracteres corresponde</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-448">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-449">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-449">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-450">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-450">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-451">A subcadeia de caracteres corresponde</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-451">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-452">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-452">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-453">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-453">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-454">Corresponde à expressão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-454">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-455">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-455">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-456">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-456">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-457">Não diferencia maiúsculas de minúsculas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-457">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-458">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-458">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-459">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-459">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-460">Confira `^` e `$` acima</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-460">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-461">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-461">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-462">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-462">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-463">Confira `^` e `$` acima</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-463">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-464">Para saber mais sobre a sintaxe de expressões regulares, confira [Expressões regulares do .NET Framework](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-464">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-465">Para restringir um parâmetro a um conjunto conhecido de valores possíveis, use uma expressão regular.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-465">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-466">Por exemplo, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` apenas corresponde o valor da rota `action` a `list`, `get` ou `create`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-466">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-467">Se passada para o dicionário de restrições, a cadeia de caracteres `^(list|get|create)$` é equivalente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-467">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-468">As restrições passadas para o dicionário de restrições (não embutidas em um modelo) que não correspondem a uma das restrições conhecidas também são tratadas como expressões regulares.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-468">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary (not inline within a template) that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

## <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-469">Restrições de rota personalizadas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-469">Custom Route Constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-470">Além das restrições de rota internas, é possível criar restrições de rota personalizadas com a implementação da interface do <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-470">In addition to the built-in route constraints, custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-471">A interface do <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> contém um único método, `Match`, que retorna `true` quando a restrição é satisfeita. Caso contrário, retorna `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-471">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface contains a single method, `Match`, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-472">Para usar uma <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> personalizada, o tipo de restrição de rota deve ser registrado com o <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> do aplicativo, no contêiner de serviço do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-472">To use a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the app's service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-473">O <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> é um dicionário que mapeia as chaves de restrição de rota para implementações de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> que validam essas restrições.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-473">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-474">É possível atualizar o <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> do aplicativo no `Startup.ConfigureServices` como parte de uma chamada [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) ou configurando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> diretamente com `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-474">An app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-475">Por exemplo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-475">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    options.ConstraintMap.Add("customName", typeof(MyCustomConstraint));
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-476">a restrição pode então ser aplicada às rotas da maneira usual, usando o nome especificado ao registrar o tipo de restrição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-476">The constraint can then be applied to routes in the usual manner, using the name specified when registering the constraint type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-477">Por exemplo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-477">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
[HttpGet("{id:customName}")]
public ActionResult<string> Get(string id)
```

## <a name="parameter-transformer-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-478">Referência de parâmetro de transformador</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-478">Parameter transformer reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-479">Transformadores de parâmetro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-479">Parameter transformers:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-480">Executar ao gerar um link para um <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-480">Execute when generating a link for a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-481">Implementar `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-481">Implement `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-482">São configurados usando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-482">Are configured using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-483">Usam o valor de rota do parâmetro e o transformam em um novo valor de cadeia de caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-483">Take the parameter's route value and transform it to a new string value.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-484">Resultam no uso do valor transformado no link gerado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-484">Result in using the transformed value in the generated link.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-485">Por exemplo, um transformador de parâmetro `slugify` personalizado em padrão de rota `blog\{article:slugify}` com `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` gera `blog\my-test-article`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-485">For example, a custom `slugify` parameter transformer in route pattern `blog\{article:slugify}` with `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` generates `blog\my-test-article`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-486">Para usar um transformador de parâmetro em um padrão de rota, configure-o primeiro usando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> em `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-486">To use a parameter transformer in a route pattern, configure it first using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    // Replace the type and the name used to refer to it with your own
    // IOutboundParameterTransformer implementation
    options.ConstraintMap["slugify"] = typeof(SlugifyParameterTransformer);
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-487">Os transformadores de parâmetro são usados pela estrutura para transformar o URI no qual um ponto de extremidade é resolvido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-487">Parameter transformers are used by the framework to transform the URI where an endpoint resolves.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-488">Por exemplo, o ASP.NET Core MVC usa os transformadores de parâmetro para transformar o valor de rota usado para corresponder a um `area`, `controller`, `action` e `page`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-488">For example, ASP.NET Core MVC uses parameter transformers to transform the route value used to match an `area`, `controller`, `action`, and `page`.</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller:slugify=Home}/{action:slugify=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-489">Com a rota anterior, a ação `SubscriptionManagementController.GetAll()` é combinada com o URI `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-489">With the preceding route, the action `SubscriptionManagementController.GetAll()` is matched with the URI `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-490">Um transformador de parâmetro não altera os valores de rota usados para gerar um link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-490">A parameter transformer doesn't change the route values used to generate a link.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-491">Por exemplo, `Url.Action("GetAll", "SubscriptionManagement")` gera `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-491">For example, `Url.Action("GetAll", "SubscriptionManagement")` outputs `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-492">ASP.NET Core fornece convenções de API para usar transformadores de parâmetro com as rotas geradas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-492">ASP.NET Core provides API conventions for using a parameter transformers with generated routes:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-493">ASP.NET Core MVC tem a convenção de API `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-493">ASP.NET Core MVC has the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention` API convention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-494">Essa convenção aplica um transformador de parâmetro especificado a todas as rotas de atributo no aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-494">This convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all attribute routes in the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-495">O transformador de parâmetro transforma os tokens de rota do atributo conforme elas são substituídas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-495">The parameter transformer transforms attribute route tokens as they are replaced.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-496">Para obter mais informações, confira [Usar um transformador de parâmetro para personalizar a substituição de token](/aspnet/core/mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-496">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize token replacement](/aspnet/core/mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-497">O Razor Pages tem a convenção de API `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-497">Razor Pages has the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention` API convention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-498">Essa convenção aplica um transformador de parâmetro especificado a todas as Razor Pages descobertas automaticamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-498">This convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all automatically discovered Razor Pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-499">O transformador de parâmetro transforma os segmentos de nome de arquivo e pasta de rotas do Razor Pages.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-499">The parameter transformer transforms the folder and file name segments of Razor Pages routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-500">Para obter mais informações, confira [Usar um transformador de parâmetros para personalizar rotas de página](/aspnet/core/razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-500">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize page routes](/aspnet/core/razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes).</span></span>

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-501">Referência de geração de URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-501">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-502">O exemplo a seguir mostra como gerar um link para uma rota com base em um dicionário de valores de rota e em um <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-502">The following example shows how to generate a link to a route given a dictionary of route values and a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_Dictionary)]

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-503">O <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> gerado no final do exemplo anterior é `/package/create/123`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-503">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generated at the end of the preceding sample is `/package/create/123`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-504">O dicionário fornece os valores de rota `operation` e `id` do modelo "Rastrear rota do pacote", `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-504">The dictionary supplies the `operation` and `id` route values of the "Track Package Route" template, `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-505">Para obter detalhes, consulte o código de exemplo na seção [Usar o middleware de roteamento](#use-routing-middleware) ou no [aplicativo de exemplo](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-505">For details, see the sample code in the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section or the [sample app](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-506">O segundo parâmetro para o construtor <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> é uma coleção de *valores de ambiente*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-506">The second parameter to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> constructor is a collection of *ambient values*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-507">Os valores de ambiente são convenientes de serem usados porque limitam o número de valores que um desenvolvedor precisa especificar em um contexto de solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-507">Ambient values are convenient to use because they limit the number of values a developer must specify within a request context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-508">Os valores de rota atuais da solicitação atual são considerados valores de ambiente para a geração de link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-508">The current route values of the current request are considered ambient values for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-509">Na ação `About` de um aplicativo ASP.NET Core MVC do `HomeController`, não é necessário especificar o valor de rota do controlador a ser vinculado à ação `Index` – o valor de ambiente `Home` é usado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-509">In an ASP.NET Core MVC app's `About` action of the `HomeController`, you don't need to specify the controller route value to link to the `Index` action&mdash;the ambient value of `Home` is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-510">Os valores de ambiente que não correspondem a um parâmetro são ignorados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-510">Ambient values that don't match a parameter are ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-511">Os valores de ambiente também são ignorados quando um valor fornecido explicitamente substitui o valor de ambiente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-511">Ambient values are also ignored when an explicitly provided value overrides the ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-512">A correspondência ocorre da esquerda para a direita na URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-512">Matching occurs from left to right in the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-513">Valores fornecidos explicitamente, mas que não correspondem a um segmento da rota, são adicionados à cadeia de consulta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-513">Values explicitly provided but that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-514">A tabela a seguir mostra o resultado do uso do modelo de rota `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-514">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-515">Valores de ambiente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-515">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-516">Valores explícitos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-516">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-517">Resultado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-517">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-518">controlador = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-518">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-519">ação = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-519">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-520">controlador = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-520">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-521">controlador = "Order", ação = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-521">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |
| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-522">controlador = "Home", cor = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-522">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-523">ação = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-523">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-524">controlador = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-524">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-525">ação = "About", cor = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-525">action = "About", color = "Red"</span></span>        | `/Home/About?color=Red` |

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-526">Se uma rota tem um valor padrão que não corresponde a um parâmetro e esse valor é fornecido de forma explícita, ele precisa corresponder ao valor padrão:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-526">If a route has a default value that doesn't correspond to a parameter and that value is explicitly provided, it must match the default value:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute("blog_route", "blog/{*slug}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadPost" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-527">A geração de link somente gera um link para essa rota quando os valores correspondentes de `controller` e `action` são fornecidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-527">Link generation only generates a link for this route when the matching values for `controller` and `action` are provided.</span></span>

## <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-528">Segmentos complexos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-528">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-529">Segmentos complexos (por exemplo, `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) são processados por meio da combinação de literais da direita para a esquerda, de uma maneira diferente de Greedy.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-529">Complex segments (for example `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) are processed by matching up literals from right to left in a non-greedy way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-530">Confira [este código](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) para ver uma explicação detalhada de como os segmentos complexos são combinados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-530">See [this code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) for a detailed explanation of how complex segments are matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-531">O [exemplo de código](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) não é usado pelo ASP.NET Core, mas fornece uma explicação adequada sobre segmentos complexos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-531">The [code sample](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) is not used by ASP.NET Core, but it provides a good explanation of complex segments.</span></span>
<!-- While that code is no longer used by ASP.NET Core for complex segment matching, it provides a good match to the current algorithm. The [current code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/91514c9af7e0f4c44029b51f05a01c6fe4c96e4c/src/Http/Routing/src/Matching/DfaMatcherBuilder.cs#L227-L244) is too abstracted from matching to be useful for understanding complex segment matching.
-->

::: moniker-end

::: moniker range="= aspnetcore-2.2"

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-532">O roteamento é responsável por mapear URIs de solicitação para pontos de extremidade e expedir solicitações de entrada para esses pontos de extremidade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-532">Routing is responsible for mapping request URIs to endpoints and dispatching incoming requests to those endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-533">As rotas são definidas no aplicativo e configuradas quando o aplicativo é iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-533">Routes are defined in the app and configured when the app starts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-534">Uma rota pode opcionalmente extrair os valores da URL contida na solicitação e esses valores podem então ser usados para o processamento da solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-534">A route can optionally extract values from the URL contained in the request, and these values can then be used for request processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-535">Usando informações de rota do aplicativo, o roteamento também é capaz de gerar URLs que são mapeadas para pontos de extremidade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-535">Using route information from the app, routing is also able to generate URLs that map to endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-536">Para usar os últimos cenários de roteamento no ASP.NET Core 2.2, especifique a [versão de compatibilidade](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) com o registro de serviços MVC em `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-536">To use the latest routing scenarios in ASP.NET Core 2.2, specify the [compatibility version](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) to the MVC services registration in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddMvc()
    .SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_2);
```

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-537">A opção <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.MvcOptions.EnableEndpointRouting> determina se o roteamento deve usar internamente a lógica baseada em ponto de extremidade ou a lógica baseada em <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> do ASP.NET Core 2.1 ou anterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-537">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.MvcOptions.EnableEndpointRouting> option determines if routing should internally use endpoint-based logic or the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based logic of ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-538">Quando a versão de compatibilidade é definida como 2.2 ou posterior, o valor padrão é `true`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-538">When the compatibility version is set to 2.2 or later, the default value is `true`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-539">Defina o valor como `false` para usar a lógica de roteamento anterior:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-539">Set the value to `false` to use the prior routing logic:</span></span>

```csharp
// Use the routing logic of ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier:
services.AddMvc(options => options.EnableEndpointRouting = false)
    .SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_2);
```

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-540">Para obter mais informações sobre o roteamento baseado em <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>, confira a [versão do ASP.NET Core 2.1 deste tópico](/aspnet/core/fundamentals/routing?view=aspnetcore-2.1).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-540">For more information on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based routing, see the [ASP.NET Core 2.1 version of this topic](/aspnet/core/fundamentals/routing?view=aspnetcore-2.1).</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-541">Este documento aborda o roteamento de nível inferior do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-541">This document covers low-level ASP.NET Core routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-542">Para obter informações sobre o roteamento do ASP.NET Core MVC, confira <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-542">For information on ASP.NET Core MVC routing, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-543">Para obter informações sobre convenções de roteamento no Razor Pages, confira <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-543">For information on routing conventions in Razor Pages, see <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-544">[Exibir ou baixar código de exemplo](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples) ([como baixar](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-544">[View or download sample code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples) ([how to download](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span></span>

## <a name="routing-basics"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-545">Conceitos básicos sobre roteamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-545">Routing basics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-546">A maioria dos aplicativos deve escolher um esquema de roteamento básico e descritivo para que as URLs sejam legíveis e significativas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-546">Most apps should choose a basic and descriptive routing scheme so that URLs are readable and meaningful.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-547">A rota convencional padrão `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-547">The default conventional route `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-548">Dá suporte a um esquema de roteamento básico e descritivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-548">Supports a basic and descriptive routing scheme.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-549">É um ponto de partida útil para aplicativos baseados em interface do usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-549">Is a useful starting point for UI-based apps.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-550">Os desenvolvedores geralmente adicionam outras rotas concisas às áreas de alto tráfego de um aplicativo em situações especiais (por exemplo, pontos de extremidade de blog e comércio eletrônico) usando o [roteamento de atributo](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#attribute-routing) ou rotas convencionais dedicadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-550">Developers commonly add additional terse routes to high-traffic areas of an app in specialized situations (for example, blog and ecommerce endpoints) using [attribute routing](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#attribute-routing) or dedicated conventional routes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-551">As APIs da Web devem usar o roteamento de atributo para modelar a funcionalidade do aplicativo como um conjunto de recursos em que as operações são representadas por verbos HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-551">Web APIs should use attribute routing to model the app's functionality as a set of resources where operations are represented by HTTP verbs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-552">Isso significa que muitas operações (por exemplo, GET, POST) no mesmo recurso lógico usarão a mesma URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-552">This means that many operations (for example, GET, POST) on the same logical resource will use the same URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-553">O roteamento de atributo fornece um nível de controle necessário para projetar cuidadosamente o layout de ponto de extremidade público de uma API.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-553">Attribute routing provides a level of control that's needed to carefully design an API's public endpoint layout.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-554">Os aplicativos do Razor Pages usam o roteamento convencional padrão para fornecer recursos nomeados na pasta *Pages* de um aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-554">Razor Pages apps use default conventional routing to serve named resources in the *Pages* folder of an app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-555">Estão disponíveis convenções adicionais que permitem a personalização do comportamento de roteamento do Razor Pages.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-555">Additional conventions are available that allow you to customize Razor Pages routing behavior.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-556">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:razor-pages/index> e <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-556">For more information, see <xref:razor-pages/index> and <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-557">O suporte à geração de URL permite que o aplicativo seja desenvolvido sem hard-coding das URLs para vincular o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-557">URL generation support allows the app to be developed without hard-coding URLs to link the app together.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-558">Esse suporte permite começar com uma configuração de roteamento básica e modificar as rotas, depois que o layout de recurso do aplicativo é determinado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-558">This support allows for starting with a basic routing configuration and modifying the routes after the app's resource layout is determined.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-559">O roteamento usa *pontos de extremidade* (`Endpoint`) para representar os pontos de extremidade lógicos em um aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-559">Routing uses *endpoints* (`Endpoint`) to represent logical endpoints in an app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-560">Um ponto de extremidade define um delegado para processar solicitações e uma coleção de metadados arbitrários.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-560">An endpoint defines a delegate to process requests and a collection of arbitrary metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-561">Os metadados usados implementam interesses paralelos com base em políticas e na configuração anexada a cada ponto de extremidade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-561">The metadata is used implement cross-cutting concerns based on policies and configuration attached to each endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-562">O sistema de roteamento tem as seguintes características:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-562">The routing system has the following characteristics:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-563">A sintaxe do modelo de rota é usada para definir rotas com os parâmetros de rota com tokens criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-563">Route template syntax is used to define routes with tokenized route parameters.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-564">A configuração de ponto de extremidade de estilo convencional e de estilo de atributo é permitida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-564">Conventional-style and attribute-style endpoint configuration is permitted.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-565"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> é usado para determinar se um parâmetro de URL contém um valor válido para determinada restrição de ponto de extremidade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-565"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> is used to determine whether a URL parameter contains a valid value for a given endpoint constraint.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-566">Modelos de aplicativo, como MVC/Razor Pages, registram todos os seus pontos de extremidade, que têm uma implementação previsível de cenários de roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-566">App models, such as MVC/Razor Pages, register all of their endpoints, which have a predictable implementation of routing scenarios.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-567">A implementação de roteamento toma decisões de roteamento, sempre que desejado no pipeline de middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-567">The routing implementation makes routing decisions wherever desired in the middleware pipeline.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-568">O Middleware que aparece após um Middleware de Roteamento pode inspecionar o resultado da decisão de ponto de extremidade do Middleware de Roteamento para determinado URI de solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-568">Middleware that appears after a Routing Middleware can inspect the result of the Routing Middleware's endpoint decision for a given request URI.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-569">É possível enumerar todos os pontos de extremidade no aplicativo em qualquer lugar do pipeline de middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-569">It's possible to enumerate all of the endpoints in the app anywhere in the middleware pipeline.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-570">Um aplicativo pode usar o roteamento para gerar URLs (por exemplo, para redirecionamento ou links) com base nas informações de ponto de extremidade e evitar URLs embutidas em código, o que ajuda na facilidade de manutenção.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-570">An app can use routing to generate URLs (for example, for redirection or links) based on endpoint information and thus avoid hard-coded URLs, which helps maintainability.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-571">A geração de URL baseia-se em endereços, que dá suporte à extensibilidade arbitrária:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-571">URL generation is based on addresses, which support arbitrary extensibility:</span></span>

  * <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-572">A API de Gerador de Link (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>) pode ser resolvida em qualquer lugar usando a [DI (Injeção de Dependência)](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection) para gerar URLs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-572">The Link Generator API (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>) can be resolved anywhere using [dependency injection (DI)](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection) to generate URLs.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-573">Quando a API de Gerador de Link não está disponível por meio da DI, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> oferece métodos para criar URLs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-573">Where the Link Generator API isn't available via DI, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> offers methods to build URLs.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-574">Com o lançamento do roteamento de ponto de extremidade no ASP.NET Core 2.2, a vinculação de ponto de extremidade fica limitada às ações e às páginas do MVC/Razor Pages.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-574">With the release of endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2, endpoint linking is limited to MVC/Razor Pages actions and pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-575">As expansões de funcionalidades de vinculação de ponto de extremidade estão planejadas para versões futuras.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-575">The expansions of endpoint-linking capabilities is planned for future releases.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-576">O roteamento está conectado ao pipeline do [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) pela classe <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-576">Routing is connected to the [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) pipeline by the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware> class.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-577">O [ASP.NET Core MVC](xref:mvc/overview) adiciona o roteamento ao pipeline de middleware como parte de sua configuração e manipula o roteamento nos aplicativos do MVC e do Razor Pages.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-577">[ASP.NET Core MVC](xref:mvc/overview) adds routing to the middleware pipeline as part of its configuration and handles routing in MVC and Razor Pages apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-578">Para saber como usar o roteamento como um componente autônomo, confira a seção [Usar o Middleware de Roteamento](#use-routing-middleware).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-578">To learn how to use routing as a standalone component, see the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section.</span></span>

### <a name="url-matching"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-579">Correspondência de URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-579">URL matching</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-580">A correspondência de URL é o processo pelo qual o roteamento expede uma solicitação de entrada para um *ponto de extremidade*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-580">URL matching is the process by which routing dispatches an incoming request to an *endpoint*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-581">Esse processo se baseia nos dados do caminho da URL, mas pode ser estendido para considerar qualquer dado na solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-581">This process is based on data in the URL path but can be extended to consider any data in the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-582">A capacidade de expedir solicitações para manipuladores separados é fundamental para dimensionar o tamanho e a complexidade de um aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-582">The ability to dispatch requests to separate handlers is key to scaling the size and complexity of an app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-583">O sistema de roteamento no roteamento de ponto de extremidade é responsável por todas as decisões de expedição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-583">The routing system in endpoint routing is responsible for all dispatching decisions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-584">Como o middleware aplica políticas com base no ponto de extremidade selecionado, é importante que qualquer decisão que possa afetar a expedição ou a aplicação de políticas de segurança seja feita dentro do sistema de roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-584">Since the middleware applies policies based on the selected endpoint, it's important that any decision that can affect dispatching or the application of security policies is made inside the routing system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-585">Quando o delegado do ponto de extremidade é executado, as propriedades de [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) são definidas com valores apropriados com base no processamento da solicitação executado até o momento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-585">When the endpoint delegate is executed, the properties of [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) are set to appropriate values based on the request processing performed thus far.</span></span>
