<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-586">[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values*) é um dicionário de *valores de rota* produzido por meio da rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-586">[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values*) is a dictionary of *route values* produced from the route.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-587">Esses valores geralmente são determinados pela criação de token da URL e podem ser usados para aceitar a entrada do usuário ou tomar outras decisões de expedição dentro do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-587">These values are usually determined by tokenizing the URL and can be used to accept user input or to make further dispatching decisions inside the app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-588">[RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) é um recipiente de propriedades de dados adicionais relacionados à rota correspondente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-588">[RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) is a property bag of additional data related to the matched route.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-589"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*> são fornecidos para dar suporte à associação de dados de estado com cada rota para que o aplicativo possa tomar decisões com base em qual rota teve uma correspondência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-589"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*> are provided to support associating state data with each route so that the app can make decisions based on which route matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-590">Esses valores são definidos pelo desenvolvedor e **não** afetam de forma alguma o comportamento do roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-590">These values are developer-defined and do **not** affect the behavior of routing in any way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-591">Além disso, os valores em stash em [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) podem ser de qualquer tipo, ao contrário de [RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values), que devem ser conversíveis de/para cadeias de caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-591">Additionally, values stashed in [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) can be of any type, in contrast to [RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values), which must be convertible to and from strings.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-592">[RouteData.Routers](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers) é uma lista das rotas que participaram da correspondência bem-sucedida da solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-592">[RouteData.Routers](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers) is a list of the routes that took part in successfully matching the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-593">As rotas podem ser aninhadas uma dentro da outra.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-593">Routes can be nested inside of one another.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-594">A propriedade <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> reflete o caminho pela árvore lógica de rotas que resultou em uma correspondência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-594">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> property reflects the path through the logical tree of routes that resulted in a match.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-595">Em geral, o primeiro item em <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> é a coleção de rotas e deve ser usado para a geração de URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-595">Generally, the first item in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> is the route collection and should be used for URL generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-596">O último item em <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> é o manipulador de rotas que teve uma correspondência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-596">The last item in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> is the route handler that matched.</span></span>

<a name="lg"></a>

### <a name="url-generation-with-linkgenerator"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-597">Geração de URL com o LinkGenerator</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-597">URL generation with LinkGenerator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-598">Geração de URL é o processo pelo qual o roteamento pode criar um caminho de URL de acordo com um conjunto de valores de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-598">URL generation is the process by which routing can create a URL path based on a set of route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-599">Isso permite uma separação lógica entre os pontos de extremidade e as URLs que os acessam.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-599">This allows for a logical separation between your endpoints and the URLs that access them.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-600">O roteamento de ponto de extremidade inclui a API de Gerador de Link (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-600">Endpoint routing includes the Link Generator API (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-601"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> é um serviço singleton que pode ser recuperado por meio da DI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-601"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> is a singleton service that can be retrieved from DI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-602">A API pode ser usada fora do contexto de uma solicitação em execução.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-602">The API can be used outside of the context of an executing request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-603"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> do MVC e cenários que dependem de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>, como [Auxiliares de Marcação](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro), Auxiliares de HTML e [Resultados da Ação](xref:mvc/controllers/actions), usam o gerador de link para fornecer funcionalidades de geração de link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-603">MVC's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> and scenarios that rely on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>, such as [Tag Helpers](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro), HTML Helpers, and [Action Results](xref:mvc/controllers/actions), use the link generator to provide link generating capabilities.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-604">O gerador de link é respaldado pelo conceito de um *endereço* e *esquemas de endereço*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-604">The link generator is backed by the concept of an *address* and *address schemes*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-605">Um esquema de endereço é uma maneira de determinar os pontos de extremidade que devem ser considerados para a geração de link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-605">An address scheme is a way of determining the endpoints that should be considered for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-606">Por exemplo, os cenários de nome de rota e valores de rota com os quais muitos usuários estão familiarizados no MVC/Razor Pages são implementados como um esquema de endereço.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-606">For example, the route name and route values scenarios many users are familiar with from MVC/Razor Pages are implemented as an address scheme.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-607">O gerador de link pode ser vinculado a ações e páginas do MVC/Razor Pages por meio dos seguintes métodos de extensão:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-607">The link generator can link to MVC/Razor Pages actions and pages via the following extension methods:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByPage*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByPage*>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-608">Uma sobrecarga desses métodos aceita argumentos que incluem o `HttpContext`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-608">An overload of these methods accepts arguments that include the `HttpContext`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-609">Esses métodos são funcionalmente equivalentes a `Url.Action` e `Url.Page`, mas oferecem mais flexibilidade e opções.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-609">These methods are functionally equivalent to `Url.Action` and `Url.Page` but offer additional flexibility and options.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-610">Os métodos `GetPath*` são mais semelhantes a `Url.Action` e `Url.Page`, pois geram um URI que contém um caminho absoluto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-610">The `GetPath*` methods are most similar to `Url.Action` and `Url.Page` in that they generate a URI containing an absolute path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-611">Os métodos `GetUri*` sempre geram um URI absoluto que contém um esquema e um host.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-611">The `GetUri*` methods always generate an absolute URI containing a scheme and host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-612">Os métodos que aceitam um `HttpContext` geram um URI no contexto da solicitação em execução.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-612">The methods that accept an `HttpContext` generate a URI in the context of the executing request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-613">Os valores de rota de ambiente, o caminho base da URL, o esquema e o host da solicitação em execução são usados, a menos que sejam substituídos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-613">The ambient route values, URL base path, scheme, and host from the executing request are used unless overridden.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-614"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> é chamado com um endereço.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-614"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> is called with an address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-615">A geração de um URI ocorre em duas etapas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-615">Generating a URI occurs in two steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-616">Um endereço é associado a uma lista de pontos de extremidade que correspondem ao endereço.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-616">An address is bound to a list of endpoints that match the address.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-617">O `RoutePattern` de cada ponto de extremidade é avaliado até que seja encontrado um padrão de rota correspondente aos valores fornecidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-617">Each endpoint's `RoutePattern` is evaluated until a route pattern that matches the supplied values is found.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-618">A saída resultante é combinada com as outras partes de URI fornecidas ao gerador de link e é retornada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-618">The resulting output is combined with the other URI parts supplied to the link generator and returned.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-619">Os métodos fornecidos pelo <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> dão suporte a funcionalidades de geração de link padrão para qualquer tipo de endereço.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-619">The methods provided by <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> support standard link generation capabilities for any type of address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-620">A maneira mais conveniente usar o gerador de link é por meio de métodos de extensão que executam operações para um tipo de endereço específico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-620">The most convenient way to use the link generator is through extension methods that perform operations for a specific address type.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-621">Método de extensão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-621">Extension Method</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-622">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-622">Description</span></span>                                                         |
| ------------------ | ------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-623">Gera um URI com um caminho absoluto com base nos valores fornecidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-623">Generates a URI with an absolute path based on the provided values.</span></span> |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetUriByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-624">Gera um URI absoluto com base nos valores fornecidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-624">Generates an absolute URI based on the provided values.</span></span>             |

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-625">Preste atenção às seguintes implicações da chamada de métodos <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-625">Pay attention to the following implications of calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> methods:</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-626">Use métodos de extensão de `GetUri*` com cuidado em uma configuração de aplicativo que não valide o cabeçalho `Host` das solicitações de entrada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-626">Use `GetUri*` extension methods with caution in an app configuration that doesn't validate the `Host` header of incoming requests.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-627">Se o cabeçalho `Host` das solicitações de entrada não é validado, uma entrada de solicitação não confiável pode ser enviada novamente ao cliente em URIs em uma exibição/página.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-627">If the `Host` header of incoming requests isn't validated, untrusted request input can be sent back to the client in URIs in a view/page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-628">Recomendamos que todos os aplicativos de produção configurem seu servidor para validar o cabeçalho `Host` com os valores válidos conhecidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-628">We recommend that all production apps configure their server to validate the `Host` header against known valid values.</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-629">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> com cuidado no middleware em combinação com `Map` ou `MapWhen`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-629">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> with caution in middleware in combination with `Map` or `MapWhen`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-630">`Map*` altera o caminho base da solicitação em execução, o que afeta a saída da geração de link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-630">`Map*` changes the base path of the executing request, which affects the output of link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-631">Todas as APIs de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> permitem a especificação de um caminho base.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-631">All of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> APIs allow specifying a base path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-632">Sempre especifique um caminho base vazio para desfazer o efeito de `Map*` na geração de link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-632">Always specify an empty base path to undo `Map*`'s affect on link generation.</span></span>

## <a name="differences-from-earlier-versions-of-routing"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-633">Diferenças das versões anteriores de roteamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-633">Differences from earlier versions of routing</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-634">Existem algumas diferenças entre o roteamento de ponto de extremidade no ASP.NET Core 2.2 ou posterior e nas versões anteriores de roteamento no ASP.NET Core:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-634">A few differences exist between endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later and earlier versions of routing in ASP.NET Core:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-635">O sistema de roteamento do ponto de extremidade não dá suporte à extensibilidade baseada em <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>, incluindo a herança de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-635">The endpoint routing system doesn't support <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based extensibility, including inheriting from <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-636">O roteamento de ponto de extremidade não dá suporte a [WebApiCompatShim](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.WebApiCompatShim).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-636">Endpoint routing doesn't support [WebApiCompatShim](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.WebApiCompatShim).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-637">Use a [versão de compatibilidade](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) 2.1 (`.SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_1)`) para continuar usando o shim de compatibilidade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-637">Use the 2.1 [compatibility version](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) (`.SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_1)`) to continue using the compatibility shim.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-638">O Roteamento de Ponto de Extremidade tem um comportamento diferente para o uso de maiúsculas dos URIs gerados ao usar rotas convencionais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-638">Endpoint Routing has different behavior for the casing of generated URIs when using conventional routes.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-639">Considere o seguinte modelo de rota padrão:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-639">Consider the following default route template:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  app.UseMvc(routes =>
  {
      routes.MapRoute("default", "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
  });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-640">Suponha que você gere um link para uma ação usando a seguinte rota:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-640">Suppose you generate a link to an action using the following route:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  var link = Url.Action("ReadPost", "blog", new { id = 17, });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-641">Com o roteamento baseado em <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>, esse código gera um URI igual a `/blog/ReadPost/17`, que respeita o uso de maiúsculas do valor de rota fornecido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-641">With <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based routing, this code generates a URI of `/blog/ReadPost/17`, which respects the casing of the provided route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-642">O roteamento de ponto de extremidade no ASP.NET Core 2.2 ou posterior produz `/Blog/ReadPost/17` ("Blog" está em letras maiúsculas).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-642">Endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later produces `/Blog/ReadPost/17` ("Blog" is capitalized).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-643">O roteamento de ponto de extremidade fornece a interface `IOutboundParameterTransformer` que pode ser usada para personalizar esse comportamento globalmente ou para aplicar diferentes convenções ao mapeamento de URLs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-643">Endpoint routing provides the `IOutboundParameterTransformer` interface that can be used to customize this behavior globally or to apply different conventions for mapping URLs.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-644">Para obter mais informações, confira a seção [Referência de transformador de parâmetro](#parameter-transformer-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-644">For more information, see the [Parameter transformer reference](#parameter-transformer-reference) section.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-645">A Geração de Link usada pelo MVC/Razor Pages com rotas convencionais tem um comportamento diferente ao tentar estabelecer um vínculo com um controlador/uma ação ou uma página não existente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-645">Link Generation used by MVC/Razor Pages with conventional routes behaves differently when attempting to link to an controller/action or page that doesn't exist.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-646">Considere o seguinte modelo de rota padrão:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-646">Consider the following default route template:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  app.UseMvc(routes =>
  {
      routes.MapRoute("default", "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
  });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-647">Suponha que você gere um link para uma ação usando o modelo padrão com o seguinte:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-647">Suppose you generate a link to an action using the default template with the following:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  var link = Url.Action("ReadPost", "Blog", new { id = 17, });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-648">Com o roteamento baseado em `IRouter`, o resultado é sempre `/Blog/ReadPost/17`, mesmo se o `BlogController` não existe ou não tem um método de ação `ReadPost`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-648">With `IRouter`-based routing, the result is always `/Blog/ReadPost/17`, even if the `BlogController` doesn't exist or doesn't have a `ReadPost` action method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-649">Conforme esperado, o roteamento de ponto de extremidade no ASP.NET Core 2.2 ou posterior produz `/Blog/ReadPost/17` se o método de ação existe.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-649">As expected, endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later produces `/Blog/ReadPost/17` if the action method exists.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-650">*No entanto, o roteamento de ponto de extremidade produz uma cadeia de caracteres vazia se a ação não existe.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-650">*However, endpoint routing produces an empty string if the action doesn't exist.*</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-651">Conceitualmente, o roteamento de ponto de extremidade não pressupõe a existência do ponto de extremidade, caso a ação não exista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-651">Conceptually, endpoint routing doesn't assume that the endpoint exists if the action doesn't exist.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-652">O *algoritmo de invalidação de valor de ambiente* da geração de link tem um comportamento diferente quando usado com o roteamento de ponto de extremidade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-652">The link generation *ambient value invalidation algorithm* behaves differently when used with endpoint routing.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-653">A *invalidação de valor de ambiente* é o algoritmo que decide quais valores de rota da solicitação em execução no momento (os valores de ambiente) podem ser usados em operações de geração de link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-653">*Ambient value invalidation* is the algorithm that decides which route values from the currently executing request (the ambient values) can be used in link generation operations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-654">O roteamento convencional sempre invalidava valores de rota extras ao estabelecer o vínculo com uma ação diferente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-654">Conventional routing always invalidated extra route values when linking to a different action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-655">O roteamento de atributo não tinha esse comportamento antes do lançamento do ASP.NET Core 2.2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-655">Attribute routing didn't have this behavior prior to the release of ASP.NET Core 2.2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-656">Em versões anteriores do ASP.NET Core, os links para outra ação que usam os mesmos nomes de parâmetro de rota resultavam em erros de geração de link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-656">In earlier versions of ASP.NET Core, links to another action that use the same route parameter names resulted in link generation errors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-657">No ASP.NET Core 2.2 ou posterior, as duas formas de roteamento invalidam os valores ao estabelecer o vínculo com outra ação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-657">In ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later, both forms of routing invalidate values when linking to another action.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-658">Considere o exemplo a seguir no ASP.NET Core 2.1 ou anterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-658">Consider the following example in ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-659">Ao estabelecer o vínculo com outra ação (ou outra página), os valores de rota podem ser reutilizados de maneiras indesejadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-659">When linking to another action (or another page), route values can be reused in undesirable ways.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-660">Em */Pages/Store/Product.cshtml*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-660">In */Pages/Store/Product.cshtml*:</span></span>

  ```cshtml
  @page "{id}"
  @Url.Page("/Login")
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-661">Em */Pages/Login.cshtml*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-661">In */Pages/Login.cshtml*:</span></span>

  ```cshtml
  @page "{id?}"
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-662">Se o URI é `/Store/Product/18` no ASP.NET Core 2.1 ou anterior, o link gerado na página Store/Info por `@Url.Page("/Login")` é `/Login/18`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-662">If the URI is `/Store/Product/18` in ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier, the link generated on the Store/Info page by `@Url.Page("/Login")` is `/Login/18`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-663">O valor de `id` igual a 18 é reutilizado, mesmo que o destino do link seja uma parte totalmente diferente do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-663">The `id` value of 18 is reused, even though the link destination is different part of the app entirely.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-664">O valor de rota de `id` no contexto da página `/Login` provavelmente é um valor de ID de usuário, e não um valor de ID do produto (product ID) da loja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-664">The `id` route value in the context of the `/Login` page is probably a user ID value, not a store product ID value.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-665">No roteamento de ponto de extremidade com o ASP.NET Core 2.2 ou posterior, o resultado é `/Login`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-665">In endpoint routing with ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later, the result is `/Login`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-666">Os valores de ambiente não são reutilizados quando o destino vinculado é uma ação ou uma página diferente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-666">Ambient values aren't reused when the linked destination is a different action or page.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-667">Sintaxe do parâmetro de rota de viagem de ida e volta: as barras "/" não são codificadas ao usar uma sintaxe do parâmetro catch-all de asterisco duplo (`**`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-667">Round-tripping route parameter syntax: Forward slashes aren't encoded when using a double-asterisk (`**`) catch-all parameter syntax.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-668">Durante a geração de link, o sistema de roteamento codifica o valor capturado em um parâmetro catch-all de asterisco duplo (`**`) (por exemplo, `{**myparametername}`), exceto as barras "/".</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-668">During link generation, the routing system encodes the value captured in a double-asterisk (`**`) catch-all parameter (for example, `{**myparametername}`) except the forward slashes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-669">O catch-all de asterisco duplo é compatível com o roteamento baseado em `IRouter` no ASP.NET Core 2.2 ou posterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-669">The double-asterisk catch-all is supported with `IRouter`-based routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-670">A sintaxe do parâmetro catch-all de asterisco único em versões anteriores do ASP.NET Core (`{*myparametername}`) permanece com suporte e as barras "/" são codificadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-670">The single asterisk catch-all parameter syntax in prior versions of ASP.NET Core (`{*myparametername}`) remains supported, and forward slashes are encoded.</span></span>

  | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-671">Rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-671">Route</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-672">Link gerado com</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-672">Link generated with</span></span><br>`Url.Action(new { category = "admin/products" })`&hellip; |
  | ------------------ | --------------------------------------------------------------------- |
  | `/search/{*page}`  | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-673">`/search/admin%2Fproducts` (a barra "/" é codificada)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-673">`/search/admin%2Fproducts` (the forward slash is encoded)</span></span>             |
  | `/search/{**page}` | `/search/admin/products`                                              |

### <a name="middleware-example"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-674">Exemplo de middleware</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-674">Middleware example</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-675">No exemplo a seguir, um middleware usa a API de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> para criar um link para um método de ação que lista os produtos da loja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-675">In the following example, a middleware uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API to create link to an action method that lists store products.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-676">O uso do gerador de link com sua injeção em uma classe e uma chamada a `GenerateLink` está disponível para qualquer classe em um aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-676">Using the link generator by injecting it into a class and calling `GenerateLink` is available to any class in an app.</span></span>

```csharp
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing;

public class ProductsLinkMiddleware
{
    private readonly LinkGenerator _linkGenerator;

    public ProductsLinkMiddleware(RequestDelegate next, LinkGenerator linkGenerator)
    {
        _linkGenerator = linkGenerator;
    }

    public async Task InvokeAsync(HttpContext httpContext)
    {
        var url = _linkGenerator.GetPathByAction("ListProducts", "Store");

        httpContext.Response.ContentType = "text/plain";

        await httpContext.Response.WriteAsync($"Go to {url} to see our products.");
    }
}
```

### <a name="create-routes"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-677">Criar rotas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-677">Create routes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-678">A maioria dos aplicativos cria rotas chamando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> ou um dos métodos de extensão semelhantes definidos em <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-678">Most apps create routes by calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> or one of the similar extension methods defined on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-679">Qualquer um dos métodos de extensão de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> cria uma instância de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> e a adicionam à coleção de rotas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-679">Any of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> extension methods create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> and add it to the route collection.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-680"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> não aceita um parâmetro de manipulador de rotas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-680"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> doesn't accept a route handler parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-681"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> apenas adiciona rotas que são manipuladas pelo <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-681"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> only adds routes that are handled by the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-682">Para saber mais sobre o roteamento no MVC, confira <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-682">To learn more about routing in MVC, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-683">O exemplo de código a seguir é um exemplo de uma chamada <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> usada por uma definição de rota típica do ASP.NET Core MVC:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-683">The following code example is an example of a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> call used by a typical ASP.NET Core MVC route definition:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-684">Esse modelo corresponde a um caminho de URL e extrai os valores de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-684">This template matches a URL path and extracts the route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-685">Por exemplo, o caminho `/Products/Details/17` gera os seguintes valores de rota: `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-685">For example, the path `/Products/Details/17` generates the following route values: `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-686">Os valores de rota são determinados pela divisão do caminho da URL em segmentos e pela correspondência de cada segmento com o nome do *parâmetro de rota* no modelo de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-686">Route values are determined by splitting the URL path into segments and matching each segment with the *route parameter* name in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-687">Os parâmetros de rota são nomeados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-687">Route parameters are named.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-688">Os parâmetros são definidos com a colocação do nome do parâmetro em chaves `{ ... }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-688">The parameters defined by enclosing the parameter name in braces `{ ... }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-689">O modelo anterior também pode corresponder ao caminho da URL `/` e produzir os valores `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-689">The preceding template could also match the URL path `/` and produce the values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-690">Isso ocorre porque os parâmetros de rota `{controller}` e `{action}` têm valores padrão e o parâmetro de rota `id` é opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-690">This occurs because the `{controller}` and `{action}` route parameters have default values and the `id` route parameter is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-691">Um sinal de igual (`=`) seguido de um valor após o nome do parâmetro de rota define um valor padrão para o parâmetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-691">An equals sign (`=`) followed by a value after the route parameter name defines a default value for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-692">Um ponto de interrogação (`?`) após o nome do parâmetro de rota define o parâmetro como opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-692">A question mark (`?`) after the route parameter name defines an optional parameter.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-693">Os parâmetros de rota com um valor padrão *sempre* produzem um valor de rota quando a rota corresponde.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-693">Route parameters with a default value *always* produce a route value when the route matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-694">Os parâmetros opcionais não produzem um valor de rota quando não há nenhum segmento de caminho de URL correspondente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-694">Optional parameters don't produce a route value if there was no corresponding URL path segment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-695">Confira a seção [Referência de modelo de rota](#route-template-reference) para obter uma descrição completa dos recursos e da sintaxe de modelo de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-695">See the [Route template reference](#route-template-reference) section for a thorough description of route template scenarios and syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-696">No seguinte exemplo, a definição do parâmetro de rota `{id:int}` define uma [restrição de rota](#route-constraint-reference) para o parâmetro de rota `id`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-696">In the following example, the route parameter definition `{id:int}` defines a [route constraint](#route-constraint-reference) for the `id` route parameter:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id:int}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-697">Esse modelo corresponde a um caminho de URL, como `/Products/Details/17`, mas não como `/Products/Details/Apples`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-697">This template matches a URL path like `/Products/Details/17` but not `/Products/Details/Apples`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-698">As restrições de rota implementam <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> e inspecionam valores de rota para verificá-los.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-698">Route constraints implement <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> and inspect route values to verify them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-699">Neste exemplo, o valor de rota `id` precisa ser conversível em um inteiro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-699">In this example, the route value `id` must be convertible to an integer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-700">Confira [route-constraint-reference](#route-constraint-reference) para obter uma explicação das restrições de rota fornecidas pela estrutura.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-700">See [route-constraint-reference](#route-constraint-reference) for an explanation of route constraints provided by the framework.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-701">Sobrecargas adicionais de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> aceitam valores para `constraints`, `dataTokens` e `defaults`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-701">Additional overloads of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> accept values for `constraints`, `dataTokens`, and `defaults`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-702">O uso típico desses parâmetros é passar um objeto de tipo anônimo, no qual os nomes da propriedade do tipo anônimo correspondem aos nomes do parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-702">The typical usage of these parameters is to pass an anonymously typed object, where the property names of the anonymous type match route parameter names.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-703">Os seguintes exemplos de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> criam rotas equivalentes:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-703">The following <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> examples create equivalent routes:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller}/{action}/{id?}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Home", action = "Index" });

routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-704">A sintaxe embutida para a definição de restrições e padrões pode ser interessante para rotas simples.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-704">The inline syntax for defining constraints and defaults can be convenient for simple routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-705">No entanto, há cenários, como tokens de dados, que não dão suporte à sintaxe embutida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-705">However, there are scenarios, such as data tokens, that aren't supported by inline syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-706">O seguinte exemplo demonstra mais alguns cenários:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-706">The following example demonstrates a few additional scenarios:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "blog",
    template: "Blog/{**article}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadArticle" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-707">O modelo anterior corresponde a um caminho de URL, como `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction`, e extrai os valores `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-707">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` and extracts the values `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-708">Os valores de rota padrão para `controller` e `action` são produzidos pela rota, mesmo que não haja nenhum parâmetro de rota correspondente no modelo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-708">The default route values for `controller` and `action` are produced by the route even though there are no corresponding route parameters in the template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-709">Os valores padrão podem ser especificados no modelo de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-709">Default values can be specified in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-710">O parâmetro de rota `article` é definido como um *catch-all* pela aparência de um asterisco duplo (`**`) antes do nome do parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-710">The `article` route parameter is defined as a *catch-all* by the appearance of an double asterisk (`**`) before the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-711">Os parâmetros de rota catch-all capturam o restante do caminho de URL e também podem corresponder à cadeia de caracteres vazia.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-711">Catch-all route parameters capture the remainder of the URL path and can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-712">O seguinte exemplo adiciona restrições de rota e tokens de dados:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-712">The following example adds route constraints and data tokens:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "us_english_products",
    template: "en-US/Products/{id}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Products", action = "Details" },
    constraints: new { id = new IntRouteConstraint() },
    dataTokens: new { locale = "en-US" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-713">O modelo anterior corresponde a um caminho de URL como `/en-US/Products/5` e extrai os valores de `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` e os tokens de dados `{ locale = en-US }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-713">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/en-US/Products/5` and extracts the values `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` and the data tokens `{ locale = en-US }`.</span></span>

![Tokens locais do Windows](routing/_static/tokens.png)

### <a name="route-class-url-generation"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-715">Geração de URL da classe de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-715">Route class URL generation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-716">A classe <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> também pode executar a geração de URL pela combinação de um conjunto de valores de rota com seu modelo de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-716">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class can also perform URL generation by combining a set of route values with its route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-717">Logicamente, este é o processo inverso de correspondência do caminho de URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-717">This is logically the reverse process of matching the URL path.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-718">Para entender melhor a geração de URL, imagine qual URL você deseja gerar e, em seguida, pense em como um modelo de rota corresponderia a essa URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-718">To better understand URL generation, imagine what URL you want to generate and then think about how a route template would match that URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-719">Quais valores serão produzidos?</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-719">What values would be produced?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-720">Este é o equivalente aproximado de como funciona a geração de URL na classe <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-720">This is the rough equivalent of how URL generation works in the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-721">O seguinte exemplo usa uma rota padrão geral do ASP.NET Core MVC:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-721">The following example uses a general ASP.NET Core MVC default route:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-722">Com os valores de rota `{ controller = Products, action = List }`, a URL `/Products/List` é gerada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-722">With the route values `{ controller = Products, action = List }`, the URL `/Products/List` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-723">Os valores de rota são substituídos pelos parâmetros de rota correspondentes para formar o caminho de URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-723">The route values are substituted for the corresponding route parameters to form the URL path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-724">Como `id` é um parâmetro de rota opcional, a URL é gerada com êxito sem um valor para `id`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-724">Since `id` is an optional route parameter, the URL is successfully generated without a value for `id`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-725">Com os valores de rota `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`, a URL `/` é gerada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-725">With the route values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`, the URL `/` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-726">Os valores de rota fornecidos correspondem aos valores padrão, sendo que os segmentos correspondentes aos valores padrão são omitidos com segurança.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-726">The provided route values match the default values, and the segments corresponding to the default values are safely omitted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-727">A viagem de ida e volta gerada pelas duas URLs com a definição de rota a seguir (`/Home/Index` e `/`) produz os mesmos valores de rota que foram usados para gerar a URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-727">Both URLs generated round-trip with the following route definition (`/Home/Index` and `/`) produce the same route values that were used to generate the URL.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-728">Um aplicativo que usa o ASP.NET Core MVC deve usar <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> para gerar URLs, em vez de chamar o roteamento diretamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-728">An app using ASP.NET Core MVC should use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> to generate URLs instead of calling into routing directly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-729">Para obter mais informações sobre a geração de URL, confira a seção [Referência de geração de URL](#url-generation-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-729">For more information on URL generation, see the [Url generation reference](#url-generation-reference) section.</span></span>

## <a name="use-routing-middleware"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-730">Usar o middleware de roteamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-730">Use Routing Middleware</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-731">Referencie o [metapacote Microsoft.AspNetCore.App](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) no arquivo de projeto do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-731">Reference the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App metapackage](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) in the app's project file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-732">Adicione o roteamento ao contêiner de serviço em `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-732">Add routing to the service container in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_ConfigureServices&highlight=3)]

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-733">As rotas precisam ser configuradas no método `Startup.Configure`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-733">Routes must be configured in the `Startup.Configure` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-734">O aplicativo de exemplo usa as seguintes APIs:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-734">The sample app uses the following APIs:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>
* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-735"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> &ndash; Corresponde apenas às solicitações HTTP GET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-735"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> &ndash; Matches only HTTP GET requests.</span></span>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_RouteHandler)]

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-736">A tabela a seguir mostra as respostas com os URIs fornecidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-736">The following table shows the responses with the given URIs.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-737">URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-737">URI</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-738">Resposta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-738">Response</span></span>                                          |
| ---------------------- | ------------------------------------------------- |
| `/package/create/3`    | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-739">Olá!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-739">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-740">Valores de rota: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-740">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3`    | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-741">Olá!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-741">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-742">Valores de rota: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-742">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3/`   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-743">Olá!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-743">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-744">Valores de rota: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-744">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/`      | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-745">A solicitação é ignorada; sem correspondência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-745">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |
| `GET /hello/Joe`       | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-746">Olá, Joe!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-746">Hi, Joe!</span></span>                                          |
| `POST /hello/Joe`      | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-747">A solicitação é ignorada; corresponde apenas a HTTP GET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-747">The request falls through, matches HTTP GET only.</span></span> |
| `GET /hello/Joe/Smith` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-748">A solicitação é ignorada; sem correspondência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-748">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-749">A estrutura fornece um conjunto de métodos de extensão para a criação de rotas (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-749">The framework provides a set of extension methods for creating routes (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareVerb*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-750">Os métodos `Map[Verb]` usam restrições para limitar a rota ao Verbo HTTP no nome do método.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-750">The `Map[Verb]` methods use constraints to limit the route to the HTTP Verb in the method name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-751">Por exemplo, veja <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> e <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-751">For example, see <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span></span>

## <a name="route-template-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-752">Referência de modelo de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-752">Route template reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-753">Os tokens entre chaves (`{ ... }`) definem os *parâmetros de rota* que serão associados se a rota for correspondida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-753">Tokens within curly braces (`{ ... }`) define *route parameters* that are bound if the route is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-754">Você pode definir mais de um parâmetro de rota em um segmento de rota, mas eles precisam ser separados por um valor literal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-754">You can define more than one route parameter in a route segment, but they must be separated by a literal value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-755">Por exemplo, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` não é uma rota válida, já que não há nenhum valor literal entre `{controller}` e `{action}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-755">For example, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` isn't a valid route, since there's no literal value between `{controller}` and `{action}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-756">Esses parâmetros de rota precisam ter um nome e podem ter atributos adicionais especificados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-756">These route parameters must have a name and may have additional attributes specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-757">Um texto literal diferente dos parâmetros de rota (por exemplo, `{id}`) e do separador de caminho `/` precisa corresponder ao texto na URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-757">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-758">A correspondência de texto não diferencia maiúsculas de minúsculas e se baseia na representação decodificada do caminho de URLs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-758">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URLs path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-759">Para encontrar a correspondência de um delimitador de parâmetro de rota literal (`{` ou `}`), faça o escape do delimitador repetindo o caractere (`{{` ou `}}`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-759">To match a literal route parameter delimiter (`{` or `}`), escape the delimiter by repeating the character (`{{` or `}}`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-760">Padrões de URL que tentam capturar um nome de arquivo com uma extensão de arquivo opcional apresentam considerações adicionais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-760">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-761">Por exemplo, considere o modelo `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-761">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-762">Quando existem valores para `filename` e `ext`, ambos os valores são populados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-762">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-763">Se apenas existir um valor para `filename` na URL, a rota encontrará uma correspondência, pois o ponto à direita (`.`) é opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-763">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing period (`.`) is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-764">As URLs a seguir correspondem a essa rota:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-764">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-765">Você pode usar um asterisco (`*`) ou um asterisco duplo (`**`) como um prefixo para um parâmetro de rota para associá-lo ao restante do URI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-765">You can use an asterisk (`*`) or double asterisk (`**`) as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-766">Eles são chamados de parâmetros *catch-all*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-766">These are called a *catch-all* parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-767">Por exemplo, `blog/{**slug}` corresponde a qualquer URI que começa com `/blog` e tem qualquer valor depois dele, que é atribuído ao valor de rota `slug`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-767">For example, `blog/{**slug}` matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it, which is assigned to the `slug` route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-768">Os parâmetros catch-all também podem corresponder à cadeia de caracteres vazia.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-768">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-769">O parâmetro catch-all faz o escape dos caracteres corretos quando a rota é usada para gerar uma URL, incluindo os caracteres separadores de caminho (`/`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-769">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator (`/`) characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-770">Por exemplo, a rota `foo/{*path}` com valores de rota `{ path = "my/path" }` gera `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-770">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-771">Observe o escape da barra invertida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-771">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-772">Para fazer a viagem de ida e volta dos caracteres separadores de caminho, use o prefixo do parâmetro da rota `**`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-772">To round-trip path separator characters, use the `**` route parameter prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-773">A rota `foo/{**path}` com `{ path = "my/path" }` gera `foo/my/path`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-773">The route `foo/{**path}` with `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my/path`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-774">Os parâmetros de rota podem ter *valores padrão*, designados pela especificação do valor padrão após o nome do parâmetro separado por um sinal de igual (`=`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-774">Route parameters may have *default values* designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-775">Por exemplo, `{controller=Home}` define `Home` como o valor padrão de `controller`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-775">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-776">O valor padrão é usado se nenhum valor está presente na URL para o parâmetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-776">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-777">Os parâmetros de rota se tornam opcionais com o acréscimo de um ponto de interrogação (`?`) ao final do nome do parâmetro, como em `id?`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-777">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name, as in `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-778">A diferença entre valores opcionais e parâmetros de rota padrão é que um parâmetro de rota com um valor padrão sempre produz um valor – um parâmetro opcional tem um valor somente quando um valor é fornecido pela URL de solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-778">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is that a route parameter with a default value always produces a value&mdash;an optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-779">Os parâmetros de rota podem ter restrições que precisam corresponder ao valor de rota associado da URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-779">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-780">A adição de dois-pontos (`:`) e do nome da restrição após o nome do parâmetro de rota especifica uma *restrição embutida* em um parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-780">Adding a colon (`:`) and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an *inline constraint* on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-781">Se a restrição exigir argumentos, eles ficarão entre parênteses (`(...)`) após o nome da restrição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-781">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses (`(...)`) after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-782">Várias restrições embutidas podem ser especificadas por meio do acréscimo de outros dois-pontos (`:`) e do nome da restrição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-782">Multiple inline constraints can be specified by appending another colon (`:`) and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-783">O nome da restrição e os argumentos são passados para o serviço <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> para criar uma instância de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> a ser usada no processamento de URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-783">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-784">Por exemplo, o modelo de rota `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` especifica uma restrição `minlength` com o argumento `10`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-784">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-785">Para obter mais informações sobre as restrições de rota e uma lista das restrições fornecidas pela estrutura, confira a seção [Referência de restrição de rota](#route-constraint-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-785">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-786">Os parâmetros de rota também podem ter transformadores de parâmetro, que transformam o valor de um parâmetro ao gerar links e fazer a correspondência de ações e páginas com URLs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-786">Route parameters may also have parameter transformers, which transform a parameter's value when generating links and matching actions and pages to URLs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-787">Assim como as restrições, os transformadores de parâmetro podem ser adicionados embutidos a um parâmetro de rota colocando dois-pontos (`:`) e o nome do transformador após o nome do parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-787">Like constraints, parameter transformers can be added inline to a route parameter by adding a colon (`:`) and transformer name after the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-788">Por exemplo, o modelo de rota `blog/{article:slugify}` especifica um transformador `slugify`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-788">For example, the route template `blog/{article:slugify}` specifies a `slugify` transformer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-789">Para obter mais informações sobre transformadores de parâmetro, confira a seção [Referência de transformador de parâmetro](#parameter-transformer-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-789">For more information on parameter transformers, see the [Parameter transformer reference](#parameter-transformer-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-790">A tabela a seguir demonstra modelos de rota de exemplo e seu comportamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-790">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-791">Modelo de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-791">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-792">URI de correspondência de exemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-792">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-793">O URI de solicitação&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-793">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-794">Somente corresponde ao caminho único `/hello`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-794">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-795">Faz a correspondência e define `Page` como `Home`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-795">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-796">Faz a correspondência e define `Page` como `Contact`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-796">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-797">É mapeado para o controlador `Products` e a ação `List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-797">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-798">É mapeado para o controlador `Products` e a ação `Details` (`id` definido como 123).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-798">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action (`id` set to 123).</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-799">É mapeado para o controlador `Home` e o método `Index` (`id` é ignorado).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-799">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method (`id` is ignored).</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-800">Em geral, o uso de um modelo é a abordagem mais simples para o roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-800">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-801">Restrições e padrões também podem ser especificados fora do modelo de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-801">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-802">Habilite o [Log](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) para ver como as implementações de roteamento internas, como <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, correspondem às solicitações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-802">Enable [Logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) to see how the built-in routing implementations, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, match requests.</span></span>

## <a name="reserved-routing-names"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-803">Nomes reservados de roteamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-803">Reserved routing names</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-804">As seguintes palavras-chave são nomes reservados e não podem ser usadas como nomes de rota ou parâmetros:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-804">The following keywords are reserved names and can't be used as route names or parameters:</span></span>

* `action`
* `area`
* `controller`
* `handler`
* `page`

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-805">Referência de restrição de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-805">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-806">As restrições de rota são executadas quando ocorre uma correspondência com a URL de entrada e é criado um token do caminho da URL em valores de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-806">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-807">Em geral, as restrições da rota inspecionam o valor de rota associado por meio do modelo de rota e tomam uma decisão do tipo "sim/não" sobre se o valor é aceitável ou não.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-807">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a yes/no decision about whether or not the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-808">Algumas restrições da rota usam dados fora do valor de rota para considerar se a solicitação pode ser encaminhada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-808">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-809">Por exemplo, a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> pode aceitar ou rejeitar uma solicitação de acordo com o verbo HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-809">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-810">As restrições são usadas em solicitações de roteamento e na geração de link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-810">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-811">Não use restrições para a **validação de entrada**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-811">Don't use constraints for **input validation**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-812">Se as restrições forem usadas para a **validação de entrada**, uma entrada inválida resultará em uma resposta *404 – Não Encontrado*, em vez de *400 – Solicitação Inválida* com uma mensagem de erro apropriada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-812">If constraints are used for **input validation**, invalid input results in a *404 - Not Found* response instead of a *400 - Bad Request* with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-813">As restrições de rota são usadas para **desfazer a ambiguidade** entre rotas semelhantes, não para validar as entradas de uma rota específica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-813">Route constraints are used to **disambiguate** similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-814">A tabela a seguir demonstra restrições de rota de exemplo e seu comportamento esperado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-814">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-815">restrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-815">constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-816">Exemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-816">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-817">Correspondências de exemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-817">Example Matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-818">Observações</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-818">Notes</span></span> |
| ---------- | ------- | --------------- | ----- |
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-819">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-819">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-820">Corresponde a qualquer inteiro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-820">Matches any integer</span></span> |
