<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1061">O modelo anterior também pode corresponder ao caminho da URL `/` e produzir os valores `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1061">The preceding template could also match the URL path `/` and produce the values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1062">Isso ocorre porque os parâmetros de rota `{controller}` e `{action}` têm valores padrão e o parâmetro de rota `id` é opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1062">This occurs because the `{controller}` and `{action}` route parameters have default values and the `id` route parameter is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1063">Um sinal de igual (`=`) seguido de um valor após o nome do parâmetro de rota define um valor padrão para o parâmetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1063">An equals sign (`=`) followed by a value after the route parameter name defines a default value for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1064">Um ponto de interrogação (`?`) após o nome do parâmetro de rota define o parâmetro como opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1064">A question mark (`?`) after the route parameter name defines an optional parameter.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1065">Os parâmetros de rota com um valor padrão *sempre* produzem um valor de rota quando a rota corresponde.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1065">Route parameters with a default value *always* produce a route value when the route matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1066">Os parâmetros opcionais não produzem um valor de rota quando não há nenhum segmento de caminho de URL correspondente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1066">Optional parameters don't produce a route value if there was no corresponding URL path segment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1067">Confira a seção [Referência de modelo de rota](#route-template-reference) para obter uma descrição completa dos recursos e da sintaxe de modelo de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1067">See the [Route template reference](#route-template-reference) section for a thorough description of route template scenarios and syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1068">No seguinte exemplo, a definição do parâmetro de rota `{id:int}` define uma [restrição de rota](#route-constraint-reference) para o parâmetro de rota `id`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1068">In the following example, the route parameter definition `{id:int}` defines a [route constraint](#route-constraint-reference) for the `id` route parameter:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id:int}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1069">Esse modelo corresponde a um caminho de URL, como `/Products/Details/17`, mas não como `/Products/Details/Apples`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1069">This template matches a URL path like `/Products/Details/17` but not `/Products/Details/Apples`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1070">As restrições de rota implementam <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> e inspecionam valores de rota para verificá-los.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1070">Route constraints implement <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> and inspect route values to verify them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1071">Neste exemplo, o valor de rota `id` precisa ser conversível em um inteiro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1071">In this example, the route value `id` must be convertible to an integer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1072">Confira [route-constraint-reference](#route-constraint-reference) para obter uma explicação das restrições de rota fornecidas pela estrutura.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1072">See [route-constraint-reference](#route-constraint-reference) for an explanation of route constraints provided by the framework.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1073">Sobrecargas adicionais de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> aceitam valores para `constraints`, `dataTokens` e `defaults`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1073">Additional overloads of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> accept values for `constraints`, `dataTokens`, and `defaults`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1074">O uso típico desses parâmetros é passar um objeto de tipo anônimo, no qual os nomes da propriedade do tipo anônimo correspondem aos nomes do parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1074">The typical usage of these parameters is to pass an anonymously typed object, where the property names of the anonymous type match route parameter names.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1075">Os seguintes exemplos de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> criam rotas equivalentes:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1075">The following <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> examples create equivalent routes:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller}/{action}/{id?}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Home", action = "Index" });

routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1076">A sintaxe embutida para a definição de restrições e padrões pode ser interessante para rotas simples.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1076">The inline syntax for defining constraints and defaults can be convenient for simple routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1077">No entanto, há cenários, como tokens de dados, que não dão suporte à sintaxe embutida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1077">However, there are scenarios, such as data tokens, that aren't supported by inline syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1078">O seguinte exemplo demonstra mais alguns cenários:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1078">The following example demonstrates a few additional scenarios:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "blog",
    template: "Blog/{*article}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadArticle" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1079">O modelo anterior corresponde a um caminho de URL, como `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction`, e extrai os valores `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1079">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` and extracts the values `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1080">Os valores de rota padrão para `controller` e `action` são produzidos pela rota, mesmo que não haja nenhum parâmetro de rota correspondente no modelo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1080">The default route values for `controller` and `action` are produced by the route even though there are no corresponding route parameters in the template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1081">Os valores padrão podem ser especificados no modelo de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1081">Default values can be specified in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1082">O parâmetro de rota `article` é definido como um *catch-all* pela aparência de um asterisco (`*`) antes do nome do parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1082">The `article` route parameter is defined as a *catch-all* by the appearance of an asterisk (`*`) before the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1083">Os parâmetros de rota catch-all capturam o restante do caminho de URL e também podem corresponder à cadeia de caracteres vazia.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1083">Catch-all route parameters capture the remainder of the URL path and can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1084">O seguinte exemplo adiciona restrições de rota e tokens de dados:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1084">The following example adds route constraints and data tokens:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "us_english_products",
    template: "en-US/Products/{id}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Products", action = "Details" },
    constraints: new { id = new IntRouteConstraint() },
    dataTokens: new { locale = "en-US" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1085">O modelo anterior corresponde a um caminho de URL como `/en-US/Products/5` e extrai os valores de `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` e os tokens de dados `{ locale = en-US }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1085">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/en-US/Products/5` and extracts the values `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` and the data tokens `{ locale = en-US }`.</span></span>

![Tokens locais do Windows](routing/_static/tokens.png)

### <a name="route-class-url-generation"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1087">Geração de URL da classe de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1087">Route class URL generation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1088">A classe <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> também pode executar a geração de URL pela combinação de um conjunto de valores de rota com seu modelo de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1088">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class can also perform URL generation by combining a set of route values with its route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1089">Logicamente, este é o processo inverso de correspondência do caminho de URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1089">This is logically the reverse process of matching the URL path.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1090">Para entender melhor a geração de URL, imagine qual URL você deseja gerar e, em seguida, pense em como um modelo de rota corresponderia a essa URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1090">To better understand URL generation, imagine what URL you want to generate and then think about how a route template would match that URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1091">Quais valores serão produzidos?</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1091">What values would be produced?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1092">Este é o equivalente aproximado de como funciona a geração de URL na classe <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1092">This is the rough equivalent of how URL generation works in the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1093">O seguinte exemplo usa uma rota padrão geral do ASP.NET Core MVC:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1093">The following example uses a general ASP.NET Core MVC default route:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1094">Com os valores de rota `{ controller = Products, action = List }`, a URL `/Products/List` é gerada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1094">With the route values `{ controller = Products, action = List }`, the URL `/Products/List` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1095">Os valores de rota são substituídos pelos parâmetros de rota correspondentes para formar o caminho de URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1095">The route values are substituted for the corresponding route parameters to form the URL path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1096">Como `id` é um parâmetro de rota opcional, a URL é gerada com êxito sem um valor para `id`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1096">Since `id` is an optional route parameter, the URL is successfully generated without a value for `id`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1097">Com os valores de rota `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`, a URL `/` é gerada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1097">With the route values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`, the URL `/` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1098">Os valores de rota fornecidos correspondem aos valores padrão, sendo que os segmentos correspondentes aos valores padrão são omitidos com segurança.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1098">The provided route values match the default values, and the segments corresponding to the default values are safely omitted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1099">A viagem de ida e volta gerada pelas duas URLs com a definição de rota a seguir (`/Home/Index` e `/`) produz os mesmos valores de rota que foram usados para gerar a URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1099">Both URLs generated round-trip with the following route definition (`/Home/Index` and `/`) produce the same route values that were used to generate the URL.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1100">Um aplicativo que usa o ASP.NET Core MVC deve usar <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> para gerar URLs, em vez de chamar o roteamento diretamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1100">An app using ASP.NET Core MVC should use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> to generate URLs instead of calling into routing directly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1101">Para obter mais informações sobre a geração de URL, confira a seção [Referência de geração de URL](#url-generation-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1101">For more information on URL generation, see the [Url generation reference](#url-generation-reference) section.</span></span>

## <a name="use-routing-middleware"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1102">Usar o middleware de roteamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1102">Use Routing Middleware</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1103">Referencie o [metapacote Microsoft.AspNetCore.App](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) no arquivo de projeto do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1103">Reference the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App metapackage](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) in the app's project file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1104">Adicione o roteamento ao contêiner de serviço em `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1104">Add routing to the service container in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_ConfigureServices&highlight=3)]

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1105">As rotas precisam ser configuradas no método `Startup.Configure`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1105">Routes must be configured in the `Startup.Configure` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1106">O aplicativo de exemplo usa as seguintes APIs:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1106">The sample app uses the following APIs:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>
* <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1107"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> &ndash; Corresponde apenas às solicitações HTTP GET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1107"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> &ndash; Matches only HTTP GET requests.</span></span>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_RouteHandler)]

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1108">A tabela a seguir mostra as respostas com os URIs fornecidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1108">The following table shows the responses with the given URIs.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1109">URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1109">URI</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1110">Resposta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1110">Response</span></span>                                          |
| ---------------------- | ------------------------------------------------- |
| `/package/create/3`    | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1111">Olá!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1111">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1112">Valores de rota: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1112">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3`    | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1113">Olá!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1113">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1114">Valores de rota: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1114">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3/`   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1115">Olá!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1115">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1116">Valores de rota: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1116">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/`      | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1117">A solicitação é ignorada; sem correspondência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1117">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |
| `GET /hello/Joe`       | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1118">Olá, Joe!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1118">Hi, Joe!</span></span>                                          |
| `POST /hello/Joe`      | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1119">A solicitação é ignorada; corresponde apenas a HTTP GET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1119">The request falls through, matches HTTP GET only.</span></span> |
| `GET /hello/Joe/Smith` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1120">A solicitação é ignorada; sem correspondência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1120">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1121">Se você estiver configurando uma única rota, chame <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*> passando uma instância de `IRouter`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1121">If you're configuring a single route, call <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*> passing in an `IRouter` instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1122">Você não precisa usar <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1122">You won't need to use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1123">A estrutura fornece um conjunto de métodos de extensão para a criação de rotas (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1123">The framework provides a set of extension methods for creating routes (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareVerb*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1124">Alguns dos métodos listados, como <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, exigem um <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1124">Some of listed methods, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, require a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1125">O <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate> é usado como o *manipulador de rotas* quando a rota corresponde.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1125">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate> is used as the *route handler* when the route matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1126">Outros métodos nesta família permitem configurar um pipeline de middleware a ser usado como o manipulador de rotas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1126">Other methods in this family allow configuring a middleware pipeline for use as the route handler.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1127">Se o método `Map*` não aceitar um manipulador, como <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>, ele usará o <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1127">If the `Map*` method doesn't accept a handler, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>, it uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1128">Os métodos `Map[Verb]` usam restrições para limitar a rota ao Verbo HTTP no nome do método.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1128">The `Map[Verb]` methods use constraints to limit the route to the HTTP Verb in the method name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1129">Por exemplo, veja <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> e <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1129">For example, see <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span></span>

## <a name="route-template-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1130">Referência de modelo de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1130">Route template reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1131">Os tokens entre chaves (`{ ... }`) definem os *parâmetros de rota* que serão associados se a rota for correspondida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1131">Tokens within curly braces (`{ ... }`) define *route parameters* that are bound if the route is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1132">Você pode definir mais de um parâmetro de rota em um segmento de rota, mas eles precisam ser separados por um valor literal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1132">You can define more than one route parameter in a route segment, but they must be separated by a literal value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1133">Por exemplo, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` não é uma rota válida, já que não há nenhum valor literal entre `{controller}` e `{action}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1133">For example, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` isn't a valid route, since there's no literal value between `{controller}` and `{action}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1134">Esses parâmetros de rota precisam ter um nome e podem ter atributos adicionais especificados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1134">These route parameters must have a name and may have additional attributes specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1135">Um texto literal diferente dos parâmetros de rota (por exemplo, `{id}`) e do separador de caminho `/` precisa corresponder ao texto na URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1135">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1136">A correspondência de texto não diferencia maiúsculas de minúsculas e se baseia na representação decodificada do caminho de URLs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1136">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URLs path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1137">Para encontrar a correspondência de um delimitador de parâmetro de rota literal (`{` ou `}`), faça o escape do delimitador repetindo o caractere (`{{` ou `}}`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1137">To match a literal route parameter delimiter (`{` or `}`), escape the delimiter by repeating the character (`{{` or `}}`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1138">Padrões de URL que tentam capturar um nome de arquivo com uma extensão de arquivo opcional apresentam considerações adicionais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1138">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1139">Por exemplo, considere o modelo `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1139">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1140">Quando existem valores para `filename` e `ext`, ambos os valores são populados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1140">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1141">Se apenas existir um valor para `filename` na URL, a rota encontrará uma correspondência, pois o ponto à direita (`.`) é opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1141">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing period (`.`) is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1142">As URLs a seguir correspondem a essa rota:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1142">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1143">Você pode usar o asterisco (`*`) como um prefixo para um parâmetro de rota a ser associado ao restante do URI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1143">You can use the asterisk (`*`) as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1144">Isso é chamado de parâmetro *catch-all*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1144">This is called a *catch-all* parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1145">Por exemplo, `blog/{*slug}` corresponde a qualquer URI que começa com `/blog` e tem qualquer valor depois dele, que é atribuído ao valor de rota `slug`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1145">For example, `blog/{*slug}` matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it, which is assigned to the `slug` route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1146">Os parâmetros catch-all também podem corresponder à cadeia de caracteres vazia.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1146">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1147">O parâmetro catch-all faz o escape dos caracteres corretos quando a rota é usada para gerar uma URL, incluindo os caracteres separadores de caminho (`/`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1147">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator (`/`) characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1148">Por exemplo, a rota `foo/{*path}` com valores de rota `{ path = "my/path" }` gera `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1148">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1149">Observe o escape da barra invertida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1149">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1150">Os parâmetros de rota podem ter *valores padrão*, designados pela especificação do valor padrão após o nome do parâmetro separado por um sinal de igual (`=`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1150">Route parameters may have *default values* designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1151">Por exemplo, `{controller=Home}` define `Home` como o valor padrão de `controller`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1151">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1152">O valor padrão é usado se nenhum valor está presente na URL para o parâmetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1152">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1153">Os parâmetros de rota se tornam opcionais com o acréscimo de um ponto de interrogação (`?`) ao final do nome do parâmetro, como em `id?`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1153">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name, as in `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1154">A diferença entre valores opcionais e parâmetros de rota padrão é que um parâmetro de rota com um valor padrão sempre produz um valor – um parâmetro opcional tem um valor somente quando um valor é fornecido pela URL de solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1154">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is that a route parameter with a default value always produces a value&mdash;an optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1155">Os parâmetros de rota podem ter restrições que precisam corresponder ao valor de rota associado da URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1155">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1156">A adição de dois-pontos (`:`) e do nome da restrição após o nome do parâmetro de rota especifica uma *restrição embutida* em um parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1156">Adding a colon (`:`) and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an *inline constraint* on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1157">Se a restrição exigir argumentos, eles ficarão entre parênteses (`(...)`) após o nome da restrição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1157">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses (`(...)`) after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1158">Várias restrições embutidas podem ser especificadas por meio do acréscimo de outros dois-pontos (`:`) e do nome da restrição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1158">Multiple inline constraints can be specified by appending another colon (`:`) and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1159">O nome da restrição e os argumentos são passados para o serviço <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> para criar uma instância de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> a ser usada no processamento de URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1159">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1160">Por exemplo, o modelo de rota `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` especifica uma restrição `minlength` com o argumento `10`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1160">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1161">Para obter mais informações sobre as restrições de rota e uma lista das restrições fornecidas pela estrutura, confira a seção [Referência de restrição de rota](#route-constraint-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1161">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1162">A tabela a seguir demonstra modelos de rota de exemplo e seu comportamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1162">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1163">Modelo de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1163">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1164">URI de correspondência de exemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1164">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1165">O URI de solicitação&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1165">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1166">Somente corresponde ao caminho único `/hello`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1166">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1167">Faz a correspondência e define `Page` como `Home`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1167">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1168">Faz a correspondência e define `Page` como `Contact`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1168">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1169">É mapeado para o controlador `Products` e a ação `List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1169">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1170">É mapeado para o controlador `Products` e a ação `Details` (`id` definido como 123).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1170">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action (`id` set to 123).</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1171">É mapeado para o controlador `Home` e o método `Index` (`id` é ignorado).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1171">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method (`id` is ignored).</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1172">Em geral, o uso de um modelo é a abordagem mais simples para o roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1172">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1173">Restrições e padrões também podem ser especificados fora do modelo de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1173">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1174">Habilite o [Log](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) para ver como as implementações de roteamento internas, como <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, correspondem às solicitações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1174">Enable [Logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) to see how the built-in routing implementations, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, match requests.</span></span>

## <a name="reserved-routing-names"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1175">Nomes reservados de roteamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1175">Reserved routing names</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1176">As seguintes palavras-chave são nomes reservados e não podem ser usadas como nomes de rota ou parâmetros:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1176">The following keywords are reserved names and can't be used as route names or parameters:</span></span>

* `action`
* `area`
* `controller`
* `handler`
* `page`

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1177">Referência de restrição de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1177">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1178">As restrições de rota são executadas quando ocorre uma correspondência com a URL de entrada e é criado um token do caminho da URL em valores de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1178">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1179">Em geral, as restrições da rota inspecionam o valor de rota associado por meio do modelo de rota e tomam uma decisão do tipo "sim/não" sobre se o valor é aceitável ou não.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1179">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a yes/no decision about whether or not the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1180">Algumas restrições da rota usam dados fora do valor de rota para considerar se a solicitação pode ser encaminhada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1180">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1181">Por exemplo, a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> pode aceitar ou rejeitar uma solicitação de acordo com o verbo HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1181">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1182">As restrições são usadas em solicitações de roteamento e na geração de link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1182">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1183">Não use restrições para a **validação de entrada**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1183">Don't use constraints for **input validation**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1184">Se as restrições forem usadas para a **validação de entrada**, uma entrada inválida resultará em uma resposta *404 – Não Encontrado*, em vez de *400 – Solicitação Inválida* com uma mensagem de erro apropriada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1184">If constraints are used for **input validation**, invalid input results in a *404 - Not Found* response instead of a *400 - Bad Request* with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1185">As restrições de rota são usadas para **desfazer a ambiguidade** entre rotas semelhantes, não para validar as entradas de uma rota específica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1185">Route constraints are used to **disambiguate** similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1186">A tabela a seguir demonstra restrições de rota de exemplo e seu comportamento esperado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1186">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1187">restrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1187">constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1188">Exemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1188">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1189">Correspondências de exemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1189">Example Matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1190">Observações</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1190">Notes</span></span> |
| ---------- | ------- | --------------- | ----- |
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1191">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1191">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1192">Corresponde a qualquer inteiro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1192">Matches any integer</span></span> |
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1193">`true`, `FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1193">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1194">Corresponde a `true` ou `false` (não diferencia maiúsculas de minúsculas)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1194">Matches `true` or `false` (case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1195">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1195">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1196">Corresponde a um valor `DateTime` válido (na cultura invariável – veja o aviso)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1196">Matches a valid `DateTime` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `decimal` | `{price:decimal}` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1197">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1197">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1198">Corresponde a um valor `decimal` válido (na cultura invariável – veja o aviso)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1198">Matches a valid `decimal` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `double` | `{weight:double}` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1199">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1199">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1200">Corresponde a um valor `double` válido (na cultura invariável – veja o aviso)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1200">Matches a valid `double` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `float` | `{weight:float}` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1201">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1201">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1202">Corresponde a um valor `float` válido (na cultura invariável – veja o aviso)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1202">Matches a valid `float` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `guid` | `{id:guid}` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1203">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1203">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1204">Corresponde a um valor `Guid` válido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1204">Matches a valid `Guid` value</span></span> |
| `long` | `{ticks:long}` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1205">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1205">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1206">Corresponde a um valor `long` válido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1206">Matches a valid `long` value</span></span> |
| `minlength(value)` | `{username:minlength(4)}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1207">A cadeia de caracteres deve ter, no mínimo, 4 caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1207">String must be at least 4 characters</span></span> |
| `maxlength(value)` | `{filename:maxlength(8)}` | `Richard` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1208">A cadeia de caracteres não pode ser maior que 8 caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1208">String must be no more than 8 characters</span></span> |
| `length(length)` | `{filename:length(12)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1209">A cadeia de caracteres deve ter exatamente 12 caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1209">String must be exactly 12 characters long</span></span> |
| `length(min,max)` | `{filename:length(8,16)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1210">A cadeia de caracteres deve ter, pelo menos, 8 e não mais de 16 caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1210">String must be at least 8 and no more than 16 characters long</span></span> |
| `min(value)` | `{age:min(18)}` | `19` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1211">O valor inteiro deve ser, pelo menos, 18</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1211">Integer value must be at least 18</span></span> |
| `max(value)` | `{age:max(120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1212">O valor inteiro não deve ser maior que 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1212">Integer value must be no more than 120</span></span> |
| `range(min,max)` | `{age:range(18,120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1213">O valor inteiro deve ser, pelo menos, 18, mas não maior que 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1213">Integer value must be at least 18 but no more than 120</span></span> |
| `alpha` | `{name:alpha}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1214">A cadeia de caracteres deve consistir em um ou mais caracteres alfabéticos (`a`-`z`, não diferencia maiúsculas de minúsculas)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1214">String must consist of one or more alphabetical characters (`a`-`z`, case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1215">A cadeia de caracteres deve corresponder à expressão regular (veja as dicas sobre como definir uma expressão regular)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1215">String must match the regular expression (see tips about defining a regular expression)</span></span> |
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1216">Usado para impor que um valor não parâmetro está presente durante a geração de URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1216">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1217">Várias restrições delimitadas por dois-pontos podem ser aplicadas a um único parâmetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1217">Multiple, colon-delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1218">Por exemplo, a restrição a seguir restringe um parâmetro para um valor inteiro de 1 ou maior:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1218">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1219">As restrições de rota que verificam a URL e são convertidas em um tipo CLR (como `int` ou `DateTime`) sempre usam a cultura invariável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1219">Route constraints that verify the URL and are converted to a CLR type (such as `int` or `DateTime`) always use the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1220">Essas restrições consideram que a URL não é localizável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1220">These constraints assume that the URL is non-localizable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1221">As restrições de rota fornecidas pela estrutura não modificam os valores armazenados nos valores de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1221">The framework-provided route constraints don't modify the values stored in route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1222">Todos os valores de rota analisados com base na URL são armazenados como cadeias de caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1222">All route values parsed from the URL are stored as strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1223">Por exemplo, a restrição `float` tenta converter o valor de rota em um float, mas o valor convertido é usado somente para verificar se ele pode ser convertido em um float.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1223">For example, the `float` constraint attempts to convert the route value to a float, but the converted value is used only to verify it can be converted to a float.</span></span>

## <a name="regular-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1224">Expressões regulares</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1224">Regular expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1225">A estrutura do ASP.NET Core adiciona `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` ao construtor de expressão regular.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1225">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1226">Confira <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> para obter uma descrição desses membros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1226">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1227">As expressões regulares usam delimitadores e tokens semelhantes aos usados pelo Roteamento e pela linguagem C#.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1227">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by Routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1228">Os tokens de expressão regular precisam ter escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1228">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1229">Para usar a expressão regular `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` no roteamento, a expressão precisa ter os caracteres `\` (barra invertida) fornecidos na cadeia de caracteres como caracteres `\\` (barra invertida dupla) no arquivo de origem C# para fazer o escape do caractere de escape da cadeia de caracteres `\` (a menos que estejam sendo usados [literais de cadeia de caracteres textuais](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1229">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in routing, the expression must have the `\` (single backslash) characters provided in the string as `\\` (double backslash) characters in the C# source file in order to escape the `\` string escape character (unless using [verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1230">Para fazer o escape dos caracteres de delimitador de parâmetro de roteamento (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), duplique os caracteres na expressão (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1230">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), double the characters in the expression (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1231">A tabela a seguir mostra uma expressão regular e a versão com escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1231">The following table shows a regular expression and the escaped version.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1232">Expressão regular</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1232">Regular Expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1233">Expressão regular com escape</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1233">Escaped Regular Expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1234">As expressões regulares usadas no roteamento geralmente começam com o caractere de acento circunflexo (`^`) e correspondem à posição inicial da cadeia de caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1234">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the caret (`^`) character and match starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1235">As expressões geralmente terminam com o caractere de cifrão (`$`) e correspondem ao final da cadeia de caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1235">The expressions often end with the dollar sign (`$`) character and match end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1236">Os caracteres `^` e `$` garantem que a expressão regular corresponde a todo o valor do parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1236">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression match the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1237">Sem os caracteres `^` e `$`, a expressão regular corresponde a qualquer subcadeia de caracteres na cadeia de caracteres, o que geralmente não é o desejado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1237">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression match any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1238">A tabela a seguir fornece exemplos e explica por que eles encontram ou não uma correspondência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1238">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1239">Expressão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1239">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1240">Cadeia de Caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1240">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1241">Corresponder a</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1241">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1242">Comentário</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1242">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1243">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1243">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1244">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1244">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1245">A subcadeia de caracteres corresponde</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1245">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1246">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1246">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1247">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1247">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1248">A subcadeia de caracteres corresponde</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1248">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1249">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1249">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1250">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1250">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1251">Corresponde à expressão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1251">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1252">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1252">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1253">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1253">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1254">Não diferencia maiúsculas de minúsculas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1254">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1255">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1255">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1256">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1256">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1257">Confira `^` e `$` acima</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1257">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1258">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1258">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1259">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1259">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1260">Confira `^` e `$` acima</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1260">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1261">Para saber mais sobre a sintaxe de expressões regulares, confira [Expressões regulares do .NET Framework](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1261">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1262">Para restringir um parâmetro a um conjunto conhecido de valores possíveis, use uma expressão regular.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1262">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1263">Por exemplo, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` apenas corresponde o valor da rota `action` a `list`, `get` ou `create`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1263">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1264">Se passada para o dicionário de restrições, a cadeia de caracteres `^(list|get|create)$` é equivalente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1264">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1265">As restrições passadas para o dicionário de restrições (não embutidas em um modelo) que não correspondem a uma das restrições conhecidas também são tratadas como expressões regulares.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1265">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary (not inline within a template) that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

## <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1266">Restrições de rota personalizadas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1266">Custom Route Constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1267">Além das restrições de rota internas, é possível criar restrições de rota personalizadas com a implementação da interface do <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1267">In addition to the built-in route constraints, custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1268">A interface do <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> contém um único método, `Match`, que retorna `true` quando a restrição é satisfeita. Caso contrário, retorna `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1268">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface contains a single method, `Match`, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1269">Para usar uma <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> personalizada, o tipo de restrição de rota deve ser registrado com o <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> do aplicativo, no contêiner de serviço do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1269">To use a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the app's service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1270">O <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> é um dicionário que mapeia as chaves de restrição de rota para implementações de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> que validam essas restrições.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1270">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1271">É possível atualizar o <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> do aplicativo no `Startup.ConfigureServices` como parte de uma chamada [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) ou configurando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> diretamente com `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1271">An app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1272">Por exemplo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1272">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    options.ConstraintMap.Add("customName", typeof(MyCustomConstraint));
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1273">a restrição pode então ser aplicada às rotas da maneira usual, usando o nome especificado ao registrar o tipo de restrição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1273">The constraint can then be applied to routes in the usual manner, using the name specified when registering the constraint type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1274">Por exemplo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1274">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
[HttpGet("{id:customName}")]
public ActionResult<string> Get(string id)
```

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1275">Referência de geração de URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1275">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1276">O exemplo a seguir mostra como gerar um link para uma rota com base em um dicionário de valores de rota e em um <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1276">The following example shows how to generate a link to a route given a dictionary of route values and a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_Dictionary)]

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1277">O <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> gerado no final do exemplo anterior é `/package/create/123`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1277">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generated at the end of the preceding sample is `/package/create/123`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1278">O dicionário fornece os valores de rota `operation` e `id` do modelo "Rastrear rota do pacote", `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1278">The dictionary supplies the `operation` and `id` route values of the "Track Package Route" template, `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1279">Para obter detalhes, consulte o código de exemplo na seção [Usar o middleware de roteamento](#use-routing-middleware) ou no [aplicativo de exemplo](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1279">For details, see the sample code in the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section or the [sample app](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1280">O segundo parâmetro para o construtor <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> é uma coleção de *valores de ambiente*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1280">The second parameter to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> constructor is a collection of *ambient values*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1281">Os valores de ambiente são convenientes de serem usados porque limitam o número de valores que um desenvolvedor precisa especificar em um contexto de solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1281">Ambient values are convenient to use because they limit the number of values a developer must specify within a request context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1282">Os valores de rota atuais da solicitação atual são considerados valores de ambiente para a geração de link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1282">The current route values of the current request are considered ambient values for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1283">Na ação `About` de um aplicativo ASP.NET Core MVC do `HomeController`, não é necessário especificar o valor de rota do controlador a ser vinculado à ação `Index` – o valor de ambiente `Home` é usado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1283">In an ASP.NET Core MVC app's `About` action of the `HomeController`, you don't need to specify the controller route value to link to the `Index` action&mdash;the ambient value of `Home` is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1284">Os valores de ambiente que não correspondem a um parâmetro são ignorados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1284">Ambient values that don't match a parameter are ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1285">Os valores de ambiente também são ignorados quando um valor fornecido explicitamente substitui o valor de ambiente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1285">Ambient values are also ignored when an explicitly provided value overrides the ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1286">A correspondência ocorre da esquerda para a direita na URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1286">Matching occurs from left to right in the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1287">Valores fornecidos explicitamente, mas que não correspondem a um segmento da rota, são adicionados à cadeia de consulta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1287">Values explicitly provided but that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1288">A tabela a seguir mostra o resultado do uso do modelo de rota `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1288">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1289">Valores de ambiente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1289">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1290">Valores explícitos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1290">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1291">Resultado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1291">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1292">controlador = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1292">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1293">ação = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1293">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1294">controlador = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1294">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1295">controlador = "Order", ação = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1295">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |
| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1296">controlador = "Home", cor = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1296">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1297">ação = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1297">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1298">controlador = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1298">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1299">ação = "About", cor = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1299">action = "About", color = "Red"</span></span>        | `/Home/About?color=Red` |

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1300">Se uma rota tem um valor padrão que não corresponde a um parâmetro e esse valor é fornecido de forma explícita, ele precisa corresponder ao valor padrão:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1300">If a route has a default value that doesn't correspond to a parameter and that value is explicitly provided, it must match the default value:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute("blog_route", "blog/{*slug}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadPost" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1301">A geração de link somente gera um link para essa rota quando os valores correspondentes de `controller` e `action` são fornecidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1301">Link generation only generates a link for this route when the matching values for `controller` and `action` are provided.</span></span>

## <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1302">Segmentos complexos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1302">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1303">Segmentos complexos (por exemplo, `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) são processados por meio da combinação de literais da direita para a esquerda, de uma maneira diferente de Greedy.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1303">Complex segments (for example `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) are processed by matching up literals from right to left in a non-greedy way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1304">Confira [este código](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) para ver uma explicação detalhada de como os segmentos complexos são combinados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1304">See [this code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) for a detailed explanation of how complex segments are matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a12bc-1305">O [exemplo de código](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) não é usado pelo ASP.NET Core, mas fornece uma explicação adequada sobre segmentos complexos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a12bc-1305">The [code sample](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) is not used by ASP.NET Core, but it provides a good explanation of complex segments.</span></span>
